Current Affairs Commentary

The Rent Reduction Movement and the Housing Problem 44

— Liu

The demand for rent reduction has a long history. Initially, tenants and landlords formed their own alliances, creating a confrontational situation. After the January 28th Incident, the Shanghai market experienced significant changes. The demand for rent reduction became even more urgent. By last year, panic was palpable, and various industries were in a slump. Maintaining livelihoods became increasingly difficult. Yet, rents remained unchanged from the past, placing an invisible burden on people. In recent years, some property owners have voluntarily reduced rents, but the recent "Rent Reduction Movement Week" suggests that there is still a sense of helplessness. Let us examine the general living conditions to discuss ways to solve the housing problem.

Everyone knows that the housing problem in Shanghai is unreasonable. The so-called "pigeon coop" style housing is generally recognized. The poor living in shantytowns live in unsanitary, damp, and filthy conditions. Shanghai's housing situation ranges from ancient cave dwellings to new 20th-century architecture. Few can enjoy a "grassland" lifestyle. Even those living in single-family homes are a minority. An examination of the household registration survey by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau reveals this. According to the Shanghai household registration survey in July of this year (excluding the Special District), there are 187,053 primary households and 226,723 secondary households. Numerically, there are 39,670 more secondary households than primary households. In terms of ratio, secondary households make up 121.2% of primary households. Breaking it down by district is even more revealing. The following table uses the number of primary households in each police precinct as a percentage and shows the ratio of secondary households to demonstrate the proportion of primary to secondary households.

1. Jiangwan Wusong Area

City Center 42.4% Wusong 71.3% Yunzaobang 46.8% Jiangwan 93.6%

2. Northern Shanghai Area

Xinzha 13.7% Menggu Road 157.6% Hengfeng Road 197.2% Zhenru 65.3%

North Station 143.3% North Sichuan Road 186.4% Yongxing Road 257.8% Linping Road 34.7%

Yinxiang Port 178.5%

3. Western Shanghai Area

Caosongdu 128.2% Pusong 39.2% Xujiahui 90.0% Caojing 87.1%

4. Southern Shanghai Area

West Gate 129.6% Old North Gate 13.1% Wenmiao Road 142.2% Shiliupu 125.9%

Dongjiadu 160.6% Yimiao 193.7% Xundao Street 167.9%

5. Pudong Area

Pudong 23.4% Yangjiadu 68.7% Yangjing 60.3% Tangqiao 61.1%

Yangsi 66.4% Gaoqiao 19.6% Donggou 29.3%

From the above table, it can be seen that the more prosperous the city, the greater the proportion of secondary households. Wusong, Jiangwan, and Pudong are not as prosperous as Western Shanghai. However, within Pudong, the ratio of secondary households in Pudong is 113.4%, while in Gaoqiao, it is only 19.6%. Although Western Shanghai is prosperous, it is not as much as Southern and Northern Shanghai. This is because part of Western Shanghai is a residential area for wealthy Chinese and foreign merchants, so there are fewer secondary households. Southern and Northern Shanghai rely on their original markets, which have increased over the years. The population is flourishing, making them the leaders of the Chinese areas. Therefore, the proportion of secondary households has also gradually increased. In the areas managed by the Yongxing Road and Linping Road police stations in Northern Shanghai and the Old North Gate police station in Southern Shanghai, there are more than two secondary households per primary household. On average, there is more than one. The density of the population in the Special District is even higher than in the Chinese areas. Except for a few residential areas for the middle class and above, the trend of subletting is rampant due to high rents. Therefore, if there were accurate figures for secondary households, the percentage would certainly be greater than in the Chinese areas. To be crammed into a small room, to eat, cook, live, sleep, to hear the crying and laughter of children, to receive guests, to work hard all day long, and yet to have such limited space for recovery and rest is a truly pitiful life for urban residents.

If this is due to a lack of housing, then the supply should be increased, and housing prices should be leveled so that the general public can enjoy a more reasonable "decent" life. If the "pigeon coop" lifestyle is due to high rents, then rent should be reduced to alleviate their hardship. There is no such thing as a rent reduction. When everything else is cheap, but rent alone is expensive, it is not fair. It should be reduced in line with general prices. The causes of high rents are: (1) the land and housing prices were pushed up by the speculative tide of the Republic of China's tenth year; (2) the high cost of imported building materials was used as an excuse due to the high value of gold and the low value of silver in previous years; (3) real estate transactions became extremely speculative; (4) landlords deliberately focused on the novelty of architectural styles to extract high rents. As a result, only the middle class and above can cope, while everyone below is oppressed by "high rents." Since rents could be increased in the past due to certain circumstances, why can't they be reduced now due to certain circumstances? Even for the landlords, if they want to revive the real estate industry, it cannot be solved by issuing circulation vouchers or establishing exchanges. Real estate must have new value before transactions can be revived. This new value must start with revising rents. Because rent revision can make those with financial resources believe that they can maintain the lowest return on their investment, and then transactions can be expected to be smooth. Therefore, a fair rent reduction is not only a blessing for tenants but also a benefit for landlords. Landlords should endure the pain for a while and make this long-term plan.

US Congress Adjourns at Midnight; Important Bills Shelved; Senator Huey Long Speaks for Seven Hours; Supplemental Appropriation Bill Fails to Pass 45

(Washington) The House of Representatives adjourned sine die at midnight, and the Senate also declared its closure five minutes later. The Third Supplemental Appropriation Bill and the amendment to the Agricultural Adjustment Act regarding cotton and wheat loans failed to pass. (National Telegram, 27th)

(Washington) Congress declared its adjournment today. Senator Huey Long made a seven-hour-long rant in an attempt to obstruct the vote. Long, who was originally a lonely and helpless figure in the Senate, used his persuasive tongue to kill the Third Financial Deficiency Relief Bill, which contained a total of $97 million for old-age pensions, retired road workers' subsidies, and the care of disabled children. Long was like a dominant demon king today. Any plea or threat to him was not enough to move him. The House of Representatives, feeling bored after adjourning, invited the US Navy Band to play music for entertainment. Later, many members of Congress flocked to the Senate to listen. The Senate then also adjourned, and Speaker Byrns read President Roosevelt's message of thanks to the legislators. Late at night, the 74th First Congress became a historical record. (National Telegram, 26th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt advocated that Congress adjourn after passing the Financial Deficiency Bill, but Senator Huey Long stood up and spoke at the last minute, disrupting the President's plan. Long claimed that he was fighting for a principle, that is, the Senate's amendment to the cotton and wheat loan was not given a chance to be voted on in the House of Representatives. The President had previously agreed to a compromise on the cotton loan, and the two houses passed a resolution to adjourn at midnight. Although the House of Representatives sent the Financial Deficiency Bill back to the Senate, the leaders of the government in the Senate asked the entire house to unanimously agree to withdraw the amendment. Long alone dissented. Majority Leader Robinson and Black denounced Long for deliberately destroying the bill that provided for disability pensions. But Long remained unyielding and shouted that he would never submit. As a result, the Deficiency Bill died due to lack of time, and the cotton and wheat amendment was also shelved. It is expected that the funds needed for social security and other programs will be allocated from the works progress funding. (Reuters, 27th)

(Washington) The 74th First Congress, which adjourned today, passed a relief bill of $900 million. If distributed equally, each American would bear $68. This is a huge sum unseen since the Great War. The most notable feature of this Congress is that none of the goals sought by the government and the New Deal faction were achieved. All legislative bills were to remedy the various bills overturned by the Supreme Court's ruling. (National Society Telegram, 26th)

US Agricultural Adjustment Administration Announces Change in Cotton Policy; Loan Increased from Nine Cents to Ten Cents 46

(Washington) The Agricultural Adjustment Administration announced tonight a change in cotton policy, increasing the government loan from nine cents to ten cents per pound. This is the result after both houses of Congress shelved the Senate's loan proposal of twelve and a half cents. (National Telegram, 26th)

(Washington) Senate Majority Leader Robinson stated today that the Agricultural Adjustment Administration's cotton loan plan has been revised, with the loan amount set at ten cents per pound, with a guarantee of twelve and a half cents for cotton farmers. This new plan requires daily calculations and payments to cotton farmers to make up the twelve and a half cents, as payments will be based on the daily average price, not the four-month average price. If so, the price obtained by cotton farmers will not be far from twelve and a half cents per pound. (Reuters, 26th)

Accomplishments of the U.S. Congress - President Signs Public Utilities Act 47

(Washington) The major bills passed during the first session of the 74th Congress include the following:

(1) Social Security Act: This law stipulates that the federal government immediately provide assistance to states to subsidize elderly paupers, while establishing a permanent national pension system. In addition, it requests that the federal government and state governments jointly establish an unemployment insurance system.

(2) Wagner-Connery Labor Disputes Act: This law stipulates that the federal government, within its legal jurisdiction, protect workers' rights to organize unions and engage in collective bargaining with employers.

(3) Banking Act: This law fundamentally reforms the existing Federal Reserve System, thereby strengthening the government's control over national lending institutions. This law imposes centralized control over the flow of credit and money, and the rediscounting of bills, while opening up various methods to facilitate credit expansion. One of the most notable points of this law is that it continues to maintain the insurance system for bank deposits.

(4) Relief Act: Authorizes the President to use $8,000,000,000 USD as unemployment relief funds, and $4,000,000,000 USD for work relief projects.

(5) Wealth Tax Act: This law increases income tax rates for annual incomes above $50,000 USD, and also significantly increases taxes on real estate and business taxes. As a result of the increased taxes under this bill, the national treasury can increase revenue by $250,000,000 USD annually.

(6) Agricultural Adjustment Act Amendment: Intended to consolidate the legality of the Agricultural Adjustment Administration.

(7) Tennessee Valley Authority Amendment: Authorizes the TVA to sell electricity to users.

(8) Air Mail Act: Stipulates the funding for opening up the Pacific air route, and also instructs the Interstate Commerce Commission to investigate whether the fees charged by the U.S. air mail service are appropriate.

(9) Transportation Act: This law places all interstate buses, trams, and trains under the management of the Interstate Commerce Commission.

(10) Recovery Act: This law stipulates that the Recovery Act be extended to April 1, 1936.

(11) Spanish-American War Veterans Act: This law fully restores the allowance payments of veterans from the 1898 war.

(12) Public Utilities Act: Although this law differs from the original proposal, it has revoked the franchises of most businesses.

(13) National Defense Act: Stipulates that $100,000,000 be used for the army and navy. The U.S. Army, which originally consisted of 163,000 men, will increase by 50,000 men under this law. In addition, several hundred aircraft and twenty-four warships will be built, and several new air force bases will be established.

(14) Extension of Agricultural Mortgage Act: This bill gives farmers some breathing room. Finally, Congress took no action on currency inflation during this session. (National News Agency dispatch, 27th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt signed the Wheeler-Rayburn Public Utility Act at 3:10 PM today. The bill has been the subject of a lengthy dispute. The Senate insisted that the provisions for cracking down on holding companies must be retained, while the House advocated for their deletion. Subsequently, a joint conference committee of the two houses agreed on a compromise solution, retaining the general principles of the Senate's original bill, which then enabled the House to accept it. Observers say that the House's acceptance was also due to the circumstances, because the President supported the compromise, and the most stringent points of the original bill had been softened, and with the congressional adjournment approaching, there was a desire to conclude the bills. As for the content of the compromise agreement, informed sources claim that the government has largely achieved the privileges it requested, but with slight modifications, so that the House leadership could offer some justification. The most important of the modifications is that the Securities and Exchange Commission has the power to decide which second-tier holding companies should be dismantled after 1938, whereas the original Senate bill stipulated that all holding companies above the first tier must be dismantled after 1942. (National News Agency dispatch, 26th)

(Washington) The Pittman Committee of the Senate, which is investigating the domestic and international impact of the Silver Purchase Act, was formally established today. The first meeting is scheduled to be held in Salt Lake City in mid-October, with the date yet to be determined. Government departments have already been requested by the committee today to provide various materials for reference at the start of the investigation. (National News Agency dispatch, 26th)

Anglo-Japanese Naval Negotiations - U.S. Expresses Indifference - Hull Says No Official News Received 48

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull stated today that the United States is not taking an active role in the Five-Power Naval Conference to be held in London in October. Hull also said that the State Department has not received any official news of developments. According to observers here, the United States has no hope of participating in any negotiations in the near future. London has not asked the United States to reaffirm its position because the United States' insistence on the Anglo-American-Japanese naval ratio has not changed to date. (National News Agency dispatch, 26th)

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull stated today that the United States is not currently actively involved in the diplomatic exchange of views between Britain and Japan regarding naval matters. He has not received news regarding submissions from Britain and Japan. Informal news is common, but Britain and Japan have not yet notified the United States with official news. Other well-informed sources here acknowledge the different positions of Britain, the United States, and Japan, and say that it is highly doubtful whether London can hold a meeting soon if Japan insists on first recognizing the principle of equality as the basis for discussion. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Britain Also Protests to Russia - Soviet Russia Has Replied with a Rejection 51

(Moscow) The British protest against the activities of Moscow Communist propagandists in Britain has been rejected by the Soviet Russian authorities. The Soviet Russian authorities seem to regard their Communist Party as unrelated to the Soviet Russian government and therefore refuse to consider this protest. It is now known that before the U.S. government sent a note to Soviet Russia on August 26, regarding the Communist Party's activities interfering in U.S. internal affairs, the governments of Italy and Latvia had also lodged similar protests. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

(London) The British Ambassador to Russia, following instructions from the British government, today drew the attention of the Russian authorities to the propaganda activities of the Moscow Communist Party in Britain. It is heard in official circles that Britain has not sent a formal document to Russia, but has only mentioned this matter in recent diplomatic conversations once or twice. Britain did not exchange views with the United States or any other country beforehand. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

(Washington) Today's U.S. protest to Russia is regarded by official and press circles here as the most strongly worded since the U.S. severed relations with Russia in 1917. It has been repeatedly stated here that the U.S. recognition of Soviet Russia at the end of 1933 was based on the following four hopes: (1) Russia would purchase U.S. heavy industry products; (2) Debts owed to the U.S. would be cleared; (3) Powerful friendly ties could be established regarding Far Eastern affairs; (4) Soviet Russia would formally supervise and control communist activities in the U.S. However, in reality, large orders have not been fulfilled, and there is still no solution to the debts owed to the U.S., and the speeches and resolutions at the recent Third International Congress have become the final straw in U.S.-Russian relations. At the same time, Soviet Russian Ambassador to the U.S. Troyanovsky said that Moscow will have a satisfactory response, and his personal opinion is that the speeches made by the American people in Moscow are but a drop in the bucket compared to the anti-Russian propaganda in the United States. According to Moscow news, Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov is currently not in the capital, and local newspapers have not mentioned a word about the U.S. protest. The Foreign Ministry is unwilling to express even informal criticism, and refuses to state when a reply can be given. (National News Agency dispatch, 26th)

Japanese Spinning Mills Import Cotton - Reaching 1,630,000 Bales 52

(Tokyo) The quantity of cotton imported by Japan, from September 1 of last year to the end of August this year, totaled 1,636,147 bales. Indian cotton accounted for the majority, with U.S. cotton slightly less. The quantity imported in the middle of this month was 1,555 bales of U.S. cotton, 36,867 bales of Indian cotton, and 2,356 bales of Egyptian cotton. Due to the increase in U.S. cotton prices, Indian cotton imports are particularly high (China Telegraph dispatch, 27th).

Reconstruction Work in Moscow 56

(Moscow dispatch, TASS, August 6) The Moscow reconstruction plan has opened up great prospects for Soviet architects' creative work. In the next ten years, various large-scale constructions will completely transform Moscow. The largest of these buildings is the Palace of Soviets, topped with a Lenin statue, 80 meters high. The height of the palace, including the Lenin statue, will reach 415 meters. Currently, the palace's designers, researchers from the Soviet Academy of Sciences, architects Iofan and Gelfreich, and Lantsere, are drafting its final plan. The cornerstone will be laid next year. The central part of the palace will have foundations reaching 30 meters deep, with a very thick layer of limestone underneath.

The Soviet Academy of Sciences is located in the center of the new Moscow district, facing the Lenin Hills. This science city has a total of 40 buildings, covering an area of 10 to 100 hectares, with a volume of 2.5 million cubic meters. The Botanical Garden nearby covers an area of 4500 hectares.

The Literary Research Institute, suggested by Gorky, is currently being designed by researcher Rylkovsky, with a volume of more than 500,000 cubic meters. A monument to Pushkin and his era will be erected in front of it.

The Central Sports Arena is currently being built in Izmailovo, a suburb of Moscow, covering an area of 300 hectares. The central grandstand of the arena can accommodate 400,000 spectators. The plan also includes establishing a sports research institute to accommodate 1,000 students. The arena also includes a team ball field, a tennis field, a shooting range, a safety parachute jumping platform, a racing track, etc. Each sports field's grandstand can accommodate 10,000 people.

The Soviet Experimental Medical College will be built on the banks of the Moscow River. The college has 10,000 rooms, of which 8,500 are various laboratories. To the left is a diagnostic room, and there is also a four-story building specifically for raising animals used in the experimental rooms. A huge "Book Hall" will be built on the corner of the Orekhovo-Zuevo Proyezd. Various publishing houses and book display areas will be moved to the hall, and a bookstore will also be established. The hall is designed by architect Golosov.

Currently, famous Moscow architects are studying street layout, embankment construction, and other building plans. These plans are all stipulated by the Moscow Ten-Year Reconstruction Plan.

French Government Meeting - To Deal with the Abyssinian Question - Laval Will Report on the Mediation Process 58

Le Journal declares that some cabinet members are demanding sanctions against Italy, while others, such as Flandin, hope to continue further cooperation with Britain. In short, France's attitude at the next League of Nations meeting will be thoroughly explained by Laval. (National News Agency dispatch, 27th)

(Paris) According to French political circles, those, especially in Britain, who are threatening Mussolini, when they read the excerpt of Mr. Mussolini's conversation published in yesterday's Daily Mail, will suddenly realize that they are wrong. This is enough to prove the legitimacy of France's opposition to imposing sanctions on Italy. French policy remains focused on limiting the scope of the Italian-Abyssinian war and maintaining friendly relations between Britain, France, and Italy as much as possible. What is especially important is to prevent the war from spreading to Europe. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

British Government Continues to Increase Defenses in the Mediterranean - Aden Port Deploys Air Defense 59

(London) The government has decided to send approximately 1,000 army personnel to Malta in the Mediterranean and Aden in the Arabian Peninsula. According to the Ministry of Aviation, these troops will carry aerial searchlights, anti-aircraft guns, and sky defense equipment. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Italian Newspapers Are Courting Japan - Recognizing That the Two Countries Have the Same Interests - Saying That They Have the Same Direction in Seeking Development and No Possibility of Discord - London Is Deeply Impressed by Mussolini's Remarks 60

(Rome) The Italian newspaper Il Giornale d'Italia carried an article today commenting on a telegram from Tokyo stating that Japan is gradually able to understand Italy's position on Abyssinia, and seized the opportunity to vigorously promote Italian-Japanese friendship. The article stated that the two countries are now pursuing development in the same direction, so there is no possibility of discord. Both countries need new land as the final destination for their increasing populations, and both are seeking natural resources that have been denied to them. After the European War, both countries felt that they were being treated with a closed door. The two countries are now encountering resistance from the League of Nations and are not allowed to enjoy the right to expand their growing populations. The problems facing Italy and Japan are of the same nature, so the two countries must seek political unity to resist their opponents. Italy's use of force in Abyssinia does not harm Japan's interests in any way, because what Italy seeks is the safety of Italians in Abyssinia and to provide Abyssinian land for the operation and trade of civilized countries, not to close the door and monopolize its benefits, and even less to close the door due to racial differences. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

(London) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's remarks to the Daily Mail yesterday made a deep impression on people in political circles here. It is believed that the British government's views on the issue of sanctions will be affected by this. Some British cabinet members believe that the proposal for sanctions is likely to expand the scope of the conflict. They originally expressed opposition, and now with Mussolini's remarks, this view is becoming stronger. The British government's proposal to strictly implement the League of Nations Covenant will inevitably be shaken slightly, but the British delegation's actions must be extremely cautious, and when the points of Italy's accusations against Abyssinia are submitted for discussion in the League of Nations Council, they must also use delaying tactics to avoid mentioning the word "sanctions." If all kinds of mediation methods ultimately fail, then the British government's final action will depend on the extent to which domestic public opinion supports or opposes the League of Nations policy. At this time, all factions in Britain are using the Abyssinian issue as discussion and propaganda material. All those who support the League of Nations and extremist left-wing groups say that the League of Nations is a symbol of democracy against dictatorship, and the British people must assist the League of Nations. Those who advocate isolation repeatedly declare, "Britain must not be dragged into the whirlpool of war." Members of the Pan-System Party are distributing leaflets advising the public to only consider British interests. In cinemas in London, especially in cinemas in suburban working-class areas, when newsreels involving the Italian-Abyssinian dispute are shown, the audience expresses disgust towards the Italian dictatorship, especially towards Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. If other newsreels involve anti-war messages, they are greeted with enthusiastic applause. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Italian Special Cabinet Meeting - The Content Is Kept Secret - Paris News Says It Discussed Financial Issues 61

(London) The Italian special cabinet meeting convened by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will be held at four o'clock this afternoon in Bolzano. The reason for convening this meeting has not been explained by Rome, which only said that administrative matters will be discussed. However, according to Paris news, the Italian Prime Minister will ask the cabinet to make an important decision on Italy's finances. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

(Rome) The news that Prime Minister Mussolini convened an emergency cabinet meeting in Bolzano on Wednesday has attracted great attention here. All ministers have gone there to participate in the army's major exercises. Political circles here say that Mr. Mussolini's move is intended to discuss various important economic and political plans to deal with the current situation. (National News Agency dispatch, 26th)

(Rome) The government is currently drafting a memorandum on Italy's reasons in the Abyssinian case, which will be submitted to the League of Nations Council meeting on September 4. It is heard that Italy advocates that Abyssinia should be expelled from the League of Nations. At the same time, political circles are keeping silent about the extraordinary cabinet meeting to be convened in Bolzano today. It is said that the meeting will only discuss administrative issues, and will not mention Abyssinia or other important issues. Mussolini is currently leading a large army in large-scale exercises in northern Italy, and has suddenly convened a cabinet meeting, probably to announce his intentions towards Abyssinia. Mr. Mussolini met yesterday with General Pes trolo, Vice-Minister of the Army, and listened to his report on the progress of the exercises. It is said that morale is excellent and the work of each team is very efficient, especially the mobile guerrilla division. The King of Italy arrived at the "front line" before dawn, got out of the car several times, inquired of officers, and had long talks with the commanders of the opposing armies. (Reuters dispatch, 27th)

(London) Minister Without Portfolio Eden and Foreign Secretary Hoare, after attending the cabinet meeting on the 22nd and 23rd, left London one after another, and are scheduled to return here this afternoon. According to news from Italy, the Italian government is currently collecting various documents, preparing to submit them to the League of Nations to accuse Abyssinia. Although officials refuse to comment on this matter, a good impression has already been formed in Britain. The general public believes that the Italian government intends to tell the world the details of what happened when the Italian-Abyssinian dispute occurred, which is consistent with what Britain advocates. It is heard that Minister Without Portfolio Eden is also preparing documents on the Italian-Abyssinian dispute and is working with the French government. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

Three Italian Navy Generals Petition the Government, Volunteering for Service; Mussolini Arrives in the North to Observe Military Exercises 62

(Rome) Three famous naval generals recently submitted a petition to the government, requesting to be assigned any task that would allow them to serve in Italian East Africa. One is Count Ciano, the former Minister of Transportation and current Speaker of the Chamber of Deputies, and son-in-law of Prime Minister Mussolini. He served as a fleet commander during the European War, stormed the port of Pola, sank an Austrian warship, and blockaded the port. The second is Vice Admiral Rizzo, and the third is Admiral Pagano, who once led a fleet into the Turkish Dardanelles Strait. In addition, the King's cousin, the Duke of Guergama, will soon go to East Africa to serve in the Italian Army's General Staff. (Havas, 26th)

(Rome) It is reported that the memorandum that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini intends to send to the League of Nations is very long, listing the hostile actions of the Abyssinians over the years, with photographs as evidence. According to Italian newspapers, Admiral Ciano, one of Italy's naval heroes in the European War, telegraphed Mussolini, requesting to be assigned to the most threatened area of Italian waters. It is said that this is in response to Britain's deployment of warships, especially in Maltese waters, which Italian newspapers are highlighting. At the same time, the army is conducting exercises in the rain in Bolzano, northern Italy. During a mock air raid last night, Mussolini was "hit by a bomb." (Reuters, 27th)

Bolzano Today in the afternoon, Prime Minister Mussolini suddenly arrived here to observe the military exercises. This is his first visit to the province of South Tyrol in twelve years of governing. After arriving, Mussolini immediately drove to the town hall to rest. As he passed through the streets, he stood up in the car, and women along the way threw flowers and kissed their hands, while men cheered and shouted, "Leader, we are willing to fight, please send us to East Africa quickly, so that we can follow in the footsteps of Vittorio and Bruno" (the names of the Prime Minister's two sons). Posters were plastered everywhere, proclaiming, "Everyone can gain glory in Africa." The main event of today's exercise was the Blue Army's attempt to concentrate its forces to capture Bolzano, while the Red Army fought hard to resist Toland. A motorized division, recently formed to replace the "Asti" division now in Africa, consisting of two infantry regiments, one machine gun battalion, one tank battalion, and one motorized artillery regiment, has arrived here to participate in the defense. It is generally believed that all of Italy's fast tanks will be equipped with 37mm cannons, according to experience gained from the exercise. (Havas, 26th)

Naples The steamship "Nazario Sauro," carrying eighty officers, 1,145 Fascist Party soldiers, and an artillery unit, set sail at 5:00 PM for the port of Massawa in Italian Eritrea, East Africa. (Havas, 26th)

Cairo The police authorities in Set Lane are on high alert, fearing that a conflict will break out between Italian Fascist Party members and anti-Italian groups when the Italian warship "Savoia" arrives in port. Mussolini's two sons and son-in-law are on board the "Savoia," and it is estimated that at least 1,000 party members will go to the port to welcome them. Anti-Italian groups have also announced that they will hold demonstrations, making conflict very likely. Transport through the Suez Canal increased sharply again at the end of the week. A total of seventeen Italian ships passed through on Saturday and Sunday, including one cruiser and one destroyer each. Abyssinia: Foreign Merchants Rush to Close Down; Banks Stop Selling Foreign Currency 63

Addis Ababa Daily life here is now clearly affected by the tense situation between Italy and Abyssinia. Foreign merchants are compiling inventories of their existing goods and submitting them to their respective embassies for record, so that they can be compensated in the event of war losses. Fourteen Greek and Italian families have been sent to the Dodecanese Islands in the Mediterranean by the Italian government. The National Bank of Abyssinia has announced that it will no longer disburse foreign currency, without specifying a time limit. The Emperor has decided to establish a consulate in the capital of the Kingdom of Yemen in the Arabian Peninsula. (Havas, 26th)

Addis Ababa The National Bank of Abyssinia refused to sell foreign exchange today. Bank officials say that this measure is not indefinite. It is generally believed that this action is another indication that Abyssinia is preparing for an imminent war with Italy. It is reported that the government stopped selling foreign exchange in order to preserve all resources and prevent capital outflow. (National Telegram, 26th)

(Paris) According to a French source in Addis Ababa, the Abyssinian Bank announced today that it has stopped selling foreign currency, apparently due to the increasing number of foreigners leaving Abyssinia. Foreigners in Addis Ababa are migrating daily, and the Italian embassy is still moving documents. Foreign shopkeepers are now compiling inventories of their goods and intend to notify their respective national embassies. At the same time, Abyssinia has decided to establish a new embassy in Yemen. (Reuters, 26th)

Addis Ababa The authorities, in view of the large number of troops and munitions being landed and unloaded in the port of Massawa, are taking even stricter precautions. Today, they ordered the procurement of military supplies and hope to build bomb shelters. Recently, the Emperor personally warned the people about how to escape in the event of an air raid. Soon, a national air defense exercise will be held, possibly as early as next week. (National Telegram, 26th)

(London) The Times received a message from the capital of Abyssinia, stating, "The Emperor ordered yesterday that three artillery rounds should be fired when enemy aircraft are not attacking. At that time, people should hide in forests and grasslands to avoid danger. After learning of this order, the people of Abyssinia believe that war is imminent. The authorities are now dispatching troops to guard the warning artillery to prevent petty thieves from issuing warning signals without authorization and taking the opportunity to loot." The newspaper also stated that the unity of Abyssinia is unprecedented. The people of the Galla region, recently conquered by the country, originally a semi-independent tribe, and the Muslims there have recently sent troops to serve the King. The southern tribes, originally conquered by Emperor Menelik, are no longer rebellious. There is a popular saying in Abyssinia: "Italian Prime Minister Mussolini thinks he has captured a docile sheep, but in reality, he has encountered a porcupine." (Havas, 27th)

European Countries: The United Socialists Should Respond to the Italian-Abyssinian War 64

(Paris) The joint committee formed by the International Federation of Trade Unions and the Second International met here to discuss the attitude to be taken towards the current situation of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. They reaffirmed the resolutions previously passed by the respective organizations, stating that the Covenant of the League of Nations and all existing treaties must be respected, and that all means of sanctions should be imposed on Italy when necessary. It was also decided to convene an extraordinary meeting of the General Council of the International Federation of Trade Unions and the Executive Committee of the Second International on September 5th and 6th to discuss a program of action. (Havas, 26th)

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: The opening was higher today due to expectations that farmers would hoard. Cotton prices are above 10 cents. The reason for the slight increase is that the government revised its lending program, stipulating that loans would be made at 10 cents per pound, with a guarantee that cotton farmers would eventually receive a price of 12 cents. This loan is suitable for cotton of 7/8 inch or longer, so the number of US cotton bales eligible for this loan will be reduced by about 200,000 bales. All cotton produced in 1935, including what has already been sold, is eligible for this program.

Impressions of a Southern Journey 80

- By Our Special Correspondent Qian Hua

(22) From Nanning to Longzhou

Longzhou is adjacent to French Vietnam and is an important border fortress in the far south. It has the Guangxi All-Border Defense and Patrol Commissioner's Office to handle border defense and diplomatic affairs, so it is the center of the province's border defense zone. The people of the country have always been very isolated from the border defense situation. Since the Northeast Incident, people of insight have gradually paid attention, but even southwestern border towns such as Longzhou are still far apart, and news is blocked. When the reporter arrived in Nanning, he planned to take a plane to inspect the border area, but unfortunately the airport was flooded, and it was not until the 16th that he took a car along the Yonglong Highway to Long. In the past, Longzhou was blocked by mountains and transportation was inconvenient. It took more than a month to reach by water, and travelers were hesitant. Recently, starting from Nanning, there is a highway by land, which only takes seven hours. By water, there are electric boats, which take two or three days when the water is high, and ten days when the water is shallow. Aviation is the Canton-Longzhou line, which only takes one hour. Education, commerce, etc. in Longzhou have gradually developed. The reporter was received by officials from the Guangxi Provincial Government. He left Nanning by car at 11:00 AM on the 16th. The entire highway is 640 li long and was built by the local militia. Although the engineering is slightly crude and the road surface and bridges are sometimes rough and uneven, and it is very easy to be damaged by floods, it is generally acceptable. Moreover, the cost is extremely low, the time is short, and the completion is rapid, which is truly commendable. There are very few plains along the entire line. Among the ten thousand mountains, the cars travel through the winding hills, and the roads rise and fall, twisting and turning. The forests are lush, and the fields are visible, as if in a wonderful landscape, forgetting the worries of the world. The car has to cross the river twice, using ferries, which takes more than an hour. Mountains protruding from the plains are everywhere. Up close, they look like rockeries made of strange stones. In the distance, they look like small islands in the sea, scattered like stars. The closer to Longzhou, the more of these strange mountains there are. Green peaks pierce the clouds, and the green is boundless, and the natural beauty is much better than artificial beauty. The car traveled for five hours to Mingjiang County. According to the person who accompanied the reception, the county town of Mingjiang was established by Di Qing when he pacified the south. His old subordinates mostly lived here and regarded themselves as descendants of meritorious officials, sitting idle and lazy to work. Bai Chongxi, Deputy Commander of the Fourth Group Army, once came here to give a speech, accusing them with righteousness. And the militia organization, all the strong men in the county had to serve in the military, and the habit of sitting idle was swept away. The population in southern Guangxi is sparse, especially in the border areas, which makes the abandoned fields along the highway all the more regrettable. Shepherds graze cattle in groups of dozens or hundreds, which proves that cattle are one of Guangxi's products. The establishment of a livestock conservation center to prevent cattle plague is especially necessary. Crossing the river from Mingjiang County to Ningming County, the mountains are heavy and the roads are even more winding. The car is also slower. When it reaches the Pingxiang County border of Longzhou, it is dark and indistinguishable from the path. It did not arrive in Longzhou until 7:30 PM and stayed at the All-Border Defense Commissioner's Office.

(23) The Border Defense Situation in Longzhou

The Guangxi border is adjacent to French Vietnam for more than 1,700 li, which is an important section of national defense in the southwest. During the Jia Shen Campaign, the fences were completely demolished. At that time, Su Yuanchun, the Guangxi Border Defense Commissioner, was honest and devoted to the country, making every effort to plan and build border defenses. The Qing court also allocated national funds to build coastal artillery platforms and barracks, deep trenches and high fortifications, and strict security. Guangxi's border defense began from this point. Since the Republic of China, the border affairs have been relaxed due to repeated turmoil. In the 21st year of the Republic of China, Li Pinxian was ordered to serve as the All-Border Defense and Patrol Commissioner, and for three years since then, he has actively reorganized border affairs, trained the militia, and resolved to let people know that we are prepared. He also adheres to a policy of good-neighborliness, with messengers coming and going, drinking and feasting together, and everything can be peaceful and tranquil on the principle of equality. After the Jia Shen War, the Regulations on Border Patrol Meetings between China and Vietnam were formulated in the 22nd year of Guangxu. The exchange between China and Vietnam was based on these regulations, which was handled by Su Yuanchun, who was also the Patrol Commissioner, who managed foreign and patrol affairs. Our side has (1) Nanguan (2) Shuikou (3) Ping'er (4) Bainan (5) Pingmeng (6) Longbang (7) Aidian (8) Nali (9) Shuolong Patrol Branch. The French side corresponding to us is (1) Siden (2) Tuolong (3) Ping'er (4) Baole (5) Shuojiang (6) Chaling (7) Zhima (8) Nashuo (9) Pingge Patrol Branch. The important task of the Patrol Branch is to jointly patrol the border with France, protect the border, and resolve disputes among border residents. At present, each patrol has a patrol police team to perform national border police duties, with more than 30 people. The Guangxi-Vietnam boundary line began to be surveyed in the 16th year of Guangxu and was completed in the 20th year. The Guangxi border was divided into east and west roads, and stone boundary markers were set up along the boundary, engraved with Chinese and French characters and marked with mileage for reference. The responsibility for the custody of the boundary markers was assigned to the respective patrol committee members and stipulated that they should be inspected once a month to see if the marker sites had been moved or the inscriptions had become blurred. Every six months, a copy of the inscription of all the boundary markers must be submitted for verification to ensure caution. At present, Longzhou has a border affairs school to cultivate specialized border affairs talents, established in the 16th year of the Republic of China. The first phase graduated in the 22nd year of the Republic of China, and after receiving military training, they were assigned to the various patrol branches for employment. After Jia Shen, Su Yuanchun built more than 100 artillery platforms of various sizes in the coastal fortresses, spending more than 5 million yuan. At present, the old rules are still maintained. Since Li took office as commissioner, he has set up factories to repair artillery platforms and other items, prepare ammunition, and dispatch soldiers to guard them separately, and send personnel to strictly inspect them at any time. As for the coastal barracks and sentry posts, many have become barren and are being repaired in stages. In addition, the coastal telephone line has also been completed, and roads can be reached everywhere. The news is sensitive, and preparations can be made quickly in the event of an alarm. At the same time, starting in November of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, the first phase of graduates from the Border Affairs School were dispatched to various coastal areas to investigate the coastal security geography, which was completed in April of the 23rd year. In the future, when national funds are abundant, there will be a way to seek for border construction.

Guangdong Province: Prospects for the Sugar Industry 81

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Guangdong Province implemented sugar industry control and established sugar factories to prevent economic loss, after the two new factories in Shitou started operation last December, the two Huizhou factories also started operation in January. Much information regarding past extraction and sales has been reported. Now that the sugarcane crushing season has passed, how will the province's sugar industry construction proceed? As it is a production-related undertaking, it should be of concern to the general public. Yesterday, the reporter conducted a detailed investigation and prepared a systematic overview for readers.

Reorganizing Sugar Factories

After the two new sugar factories in Shitou finished crushing sugarcane at the end of April this year, they actively engaged in repairing, reorganizing, and improving machinery. Therefore, all workers did not stop working. After the machinery was improved, the Shitou factory can crush more than 1,000 tons of sugarcane, and the Xinzhao factory can crush more than 500 tons. According to the last sugarcane crushing period, the Shitou factory had already been able to crush 1,100 tons, and the Xinzhao factory had also been able to crush 600 tons. If reorganization during this downtime is added, future improvements are self-evident.

Starting Sugar Refining

Sugar refining has now begun at the factories. Because there is no sugarcane to crush during this period, and because both the local market and other parts of the country have a great need for white sugar, the provincial government has specially obtained approval from the Ministry of Finance to import raw sugar according to regulations and pay taxes for use as refining material. At the same time, they are collecting local brown sugar for refining. Therefore, the two factories in Shitou and Xinzhao have recently started refining white sugar to meet the needs of this city and Shanghai. Some additional machinery was added to the refining process to produce fine granulated sugar. Currently, the two factories combined can produce 2,500 dan of sugar per day.

Improving Sugarcane Varieties

Regarding the improvement and propagation of sugarcane varieties, for several months, the focus has been on guiding sugarcane farmers to improve sugarcane planting methods and propagate superior sugarcane varieties. More than ten million superior sugarcane seedlings were imported last year. The yield of these superior sugarcane varieties is about twice that of local sugarcane varieties. After a year of testing, it is known that the Java 32878, 2883, 225, and Philippine varieties have excellent results. Trials were conducted in the Pearl River Delta in Panyu, the Chaoshan area, and Huizhou, and the results were all more productive than local varieties by more than double. Currently, the area of sugarcane fields in this province planted with these sugarcane varieties is approximately 8,000 mu, sufficient for the propagation for 120,000 mu of sugarcane fields. This year, because superior sugarcane varieties could not be propagated to the fullest extent, mostly local sugarcane was crushed. If the superior sugarcane varieties mature next year, then all superior sugarcane can be crushed. The cost of sugar can be reduced by about half, and farmers' harvests can be doubled. This is the situation of successful large-scale propagation of superior sugarcane varieties.

Contracting to Purchase Sugarcane

Last year, the two sugar factories signed contracts to purchase sugarcane. Large farmers throughout the province reported the sugarcane field area, but the actual area did not match the reported number. This year, three teams of surveyors were dispatched to accurately measure the sugarcane fields under contract in various places. According to reports, the sugarcane fields in various places were approximately 70,000 mu, but after measurement, the actual number was approximately 50,000 mu. Therefore, through this measurement, farmers cannot underreport. At the same time, the sugar factory can provide guidance for improvement, and the shortfall can be calculated and purchased in advance. This is an improvement in this year's sugarcane planting affairs.

Improving Harvesting and Transportation

Currently, there is active reorganization of last year's harvesting and transportation of sugarcane. Last year, the harvesting and transportation of sugarcane was contracted to merchants or large sugarcane farmers, so the work was not well-organized. Often, the sugarcane was not harvested and transported according to the date, delaying farmers' harvesting and transportation, and there were suspicions of extorting farmers. Methods are being developed to effectively ban this. In the future, farmers will harvest themselves, and the sugar factory will organize the transportation part to transport, no longer through the hands of large farmers, so as to avoid oppressing small farmers. Although each factory has suspended work for two months to reorganize the machinery, various tasks such as lending money for sugarcane planting and improving propagation of sugarcane varieties mean that the staff is very busy. Furthermore, sugarcane planting work takes place throughout the year. Before sugarcane crushing, the work regarding sugarcane planting, improving sugarcane varieties, guiding farmers to plant sugarcane, reorganizing transportation, refining sugar, investigating sugarcane fields, lending money to farmers to plant sugarcane, and distributing fertilizer and sugarcane varieties is extremely complicated and cumbersome, and must be handled during this period. Only when the sugarcane crushing season arrives can the sugar production work proceed quickly.

Reorganizing Huizhou Factory

The Huizhou Military Reclamation Sugar Factory planted local sugarcane last year, and because it suffered flood disasters, the quality was not very good. At the same time, the harvesting and transportation work was new, the new machinery installation was sloppy, and the staff was not very skilled. Therefore, the sugarcane crushing was slightly hindered. However, the Honolulu Iron Works Co., Ltd. is now fully responsible for repairing the machinery. When it starts operating this year, it is expected to be able to crush more than 1,000 tons. The sugarcane variety improvement in the area has also been very successful. Each mu of the new varieties can yield more than 300 dan. However, the existing sugarcane field area is very small, only 400 mu. If it can be propagated successively, except for crushing for one more year this year, all superior sugarcane varieties can be crushed next year. At that time, the benefits may exceed those of the two factories in Shitou and Xinzhao.

Preparing New Factories

Currently, the Bureau of Agriculture and Forestry is preparing for the Shunde and Chaoshan sugar factories according to the agreements. The Shunde factory is being built by the Skoda Works, and the Chaoshan factory is being built by the Honolulu Iron Works Co., Ltd. At the same time, preparations are being made to purchase sugarcane to supply the sugar factories with raw materials at the end of the year. Shunde is using the method of the First Construction Site in the Guangzhou area to lend money to farmers to plant sugarcane. The method in Chaoshan is to locally convene sugarcane merchants to organize and purchase sugarcane from farmers according to the purchase agreement and price value approved by the government to supply the sugarcane factory. It is expected that both factories can be completed on schedule, and there will be no shortage of raw material sugarcane.

Guangdong Province Eastern Border: Establishing Joint Defense Zones with Police and Guards, Organizing Joint Defense Committees in Each Zone to be Responsible for Bandit Suppression and Bandit Information Investigation 82

Recently, Guangdong Province believes that although the bandits in the neighboring provinces have been suppressed, there are still remnants of bandits gathering in the remote areas with dense mountains and forests. In order to consolidate the border, the authorities have been mobilizing military engineers to build border anti-bandit trenches, and at the same time, they have been instructing the counties along the Guangdong border to organize joint defense in various townships, conduct household registration, and investigate bandit traces to prevent bandits from infiltrating. Regarding the defense of the border areas, the Fifth and Sixth Division engineers are responsible for constructing the trenches from the Xiaobei River to the Hunan-Guangxi border, the Independent Second Brigade engineers are responsible for the trenches from the Nanxiong Xihe coast to the Jiangxi border, the Forty-First Division engineers are responsible for the highways and border trenches from Shaozhou to Wengyuan and other counties, and the Independent First Division engineers are responsible for the trenches from Jiaoling to the Fujian border. As for the eastern region, because there are still remnants of bandits from the Fujian border appearing, the military authorities, in order to carefully maintain order in the border areas, issued the joint defense regulations for the counties in the border areas yesterday. In each county in the border area, joint defense zones will be established, with two to several counties, or a certain area of a county and a certain area of a neighboring county, jointly establishing a joint defense committee, so that when there is an alarm, they can command the guard teams within the joint defense zone. The joint defense committee has one director and one deputy director, appointed by the Pacification Headquarters and the defense army commander. Recently, joint defense zones have been established in Raoping and Meixian in the eastern region. There is the Pudong Pubei Joint Defense Association, with the defense army regiment commander and Zhang Wuzhen, a member of the Dabu County Government, as the director of the Pudong Joint Defense, and Zhong Que Lian as the director of the Pubei Joint Defense. After the establishment of the joint defense zone in the area, they immediately began investigating bandit information. The investigation items are roughly as follows: (1) Bandit leader's name, (2) Number of bandits, (3) Types and number of bandit firearms, (4) Bandit gathering location, (5) Survey and map of the bandit nest location, detailing the situation and access routes, (6) Public security conditions. If there is a bandit alarm in the joint defense zone, the guard teams in the joint defense zone must cooperate in the blockade, regardless of their jurisdiction. When the defense army suppresses bandits, the guard teams in the area must also do their best to assist, so as to achieve mutual assistance between the military and the people. (August 23)

Songjiang: Case of Rape of a 15-Year-Old Girl 83

Li Jinmu, a villager in Xiaositu Township, Seventh District, Punan, has a wife, Shen, and a young daughter, Yinzhen, who is 15 years old and as precious as a gem. Yesterday, she happened to be looking after the shed when Yan Guihai, 34 years old, from the same village, passed by. Suddenly, his animalistic desires flared up, and seeing the girl, he immediately went forward, grabbed her, and forcibly pulled down her pants. The girl was frightened and cried out, and he immediately grabbed her throat, forcibly raped her, and tore her genitals, causing blood to flow like a stream. A neighbor caught a glimpse of this, and Yan immediately fled, but was caught by the neighbor. They ran to tell Yinzhen's parents, and they took Yan to the First Branch Bureau, along with a pair of bloody pants, and sent him to the Public Security Bureau for legal action.

Wuxi: Adding Interval Bus on the Wuxi-Shanghai Road 86

Since the Wuxi-Shanghai Bus Company officially opened on the 17th of this month, business at each station has been quite prosperous. The company recently found that the number of passengers getting on and off between Wuxi Station and Dongting Anzhen is extremely crowded. Seven interval buses operate daily, which is still insufficient to meet demand. It has now been decided to add six interval buses in each direction every day, with an average of one bus in each direction between the two stations of Wuxi and Anzhen every hour, starting next month. At the same time, due to competition between cars and ships between Wuxi and Anzhen, it is planned to find ways to reduce passenger fares for the Wuxi to Dongting Anzhen stations. It is also heard that the company plans to add a new car station in Chajiaqiao in this county to facilitate passengers, which will also be realized soon.

Yangzhou: Modern Girl Commits Suicide by Jumping into the River 88

The Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Automobile Company ferry Xin Zhenjiang left Liuwei for Zhenjiang at 9:40 AM today (26th). When it arrived in the middle of the river, a modern girl who had taken the ferry from Liuwei to cross the river suddenly ran from the passenger cabin to the left side and jumped into the river. At that time, the crowd shouted for help and immediately stopped the ferry and tried to salvage her. However, the girl had already gone with the waves. Upon further inspection of the cabin, only a rattan bag containing about 1,000 copper coins was left. Because there was no suicide note, her name is also unknown. The body has not yet been recovered, and the rattan bag is stored in the local Water Public Security Team.

Hangzhou: Charcoal Car Trial Competition 89

The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau is about to complete the provincial transportation network plan. The number of passengers on each road is increasing daily, and business is increasing sharply. The monthly consumption of gasoline fuel is more than 50,000 yuan. In order to implement cost reduction, it is planned to trial use charcoal cars, which is expected to save 500,000 yuan per year. Yesterday at 3:30 PM, representatives from various charcoal car companies were specially convened to hold a charcoal car trial competition. The participants included three companies: China, Zhongming, and Huaqiang. At 3:44 PM, they departed from Wulinmen Station and arrived at Moganshan. After a half-hour break, they returned to Hangzhou from Moganshan, a round trip of 116 kilometers. The competition ended at 7:00 PM. Huaqiang and Zhongming performed well, while China was slightly inferior. Huaqiang used 72.5 pounds of charcoal, Zhongming used 69 pounds, and China used 88 pounds.

Special Article

Confucius' Daily Life and Interpretation of Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Honor (Continued) 97

— H. H. Kung

Different Schools of Thought from Confucius

The School of Transmitting the Way is the ancestor of Song Learning; the School of Transmitting the Classics is the ancestor of Han Learning; the School of Transmitting Propriety belongs to the School of Transmitting the Classics; the School of Harmony between Heaven and Man is also attached to the School of Transmitting the Way and the School of Transmitting the Classics. Thus, the academic thought of China over the past two thousand years has always regarded these two schools as the two main trends. Whether they are the true learning of Confucius is still questionable. In the past (Note 12), Mr. Yan Xizhai once wanted to destroy the framework and clarify it. As for Confucius' treatment of Zilu's governance, he told him to be cautious in doing things, to like planning, and to achieve success; because of Ran You's enriching the people, he spoke of equality without poverty and harmony without scarcity; and because Zigong was a talent who could be sent in all directions, when he asked about scholars, he prioritized having shame and not being disgraced. The essence lies in this, and the foundation of the country depends on it. If showing benevolence was already shown to Yan Yuan, then expelling the barbarians still made him think of Guan Zhong. The big picture and the well-being of the people go hand in hand. The students are good at driving (such as Fan Chi driving and Ran You serving), and they should diligently study archery and chariot driving. Striving for the Way and engaging in the arts should be pursued together. And filial piety, friendship, following the law, chivalry, accumulating wealth, solitary actions, farming together, and the study of rectification of names all originated at this time. Later generations should adapt to the times, seek truth from facts, and not be like the previous moralists (pedants) and Confucian scholars (Han scholars), each claiming to be the true learning of Confucius and having the concepts of "orthodox lineage" and "academic lineage."

Note 16: Based on Chen Yushu's saying, see the preface to his Biography of Bu Zixia.

Note 2: Based on Shen Deqian's saying, see his Records of the Wu Gong Ancestral Hall.

Note 3: Based on Shao Yichen's saying, see his General Theory of the Classic of Rites.

Note 4: Based on Huang Yizhou's saying, see his Collection of Admonitions by Ji Wenzi.

Note 5: Based on Zhu Xizun's saying, see his Records of the Bu Zixia Ancestral Hall.

Note 7: Based on Feng Yunqi's saying, see his Biography of Zai Yu.

Note 8: Based on Liang Qichao's saying, see his Chinese Bushido.

Note 9: See Han Shi Wai Zhuan.

Note 10: Based on Mao Qiling's saying, see his Extraneous Words on the Four Books.

Note 11: Based on Liang Qichao's saying, see his General Trend of Changes in Chinese Academic Thought.

Note 12: Detailed in Corrections to the Four Books. (End)

Local News

Yesterday Was the Birthday of Confucius, and Various Sectors Held Commemorative Meetings 98

More than 1,000 People Attended the People's Education Center, and the Ceremony Was Grand. Various Agencies, Organizations, and Schools Raised Flags and Took a Holiday

August 27th is the nationally designated Confucius Birthday Commemoration Day. All sectors of the city held a Confucius Birthday Commemoration Meeting at 10:00 AM in the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road. More than 1,000 representatives attended, and the ceremony was particularly grand and the atmosphere was extremely warm. All agencies, organizations, and schools raised flags to celebrate and took a day off. The details of the Commemorative Meeting are recorded below:

Arrangement

The Confucius Birthday Commemoration Meeting held by representatives from all sectors of Shanghai was held in the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road, in front of the shrine of Confucius. The Party and National Flags were hung on the left and right, and the portrait of the President was hung in the middle. The portrait of Confucius was placed on the incense table in front of the shrine. In front of the portrait, there was a square table with two vases of flowers. Slogans were posted on all the pillars in the hall, and small Party and National Flags were hung in a cross shape in the air. The stage in front of the hall was occupied by the orchestra of the Commemorative Meeting and the military band of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Another Party and National Flag were hung high in front of the stage. A horizontal plaque was hung at the gate of the People's Education Center, with the words "Confucius Birthday Commemoration Meeting Held by Representatives from All Sectors of Shanghai." The Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched additional police officers to maintain order on Wenmiao Road. Several staff members from the Municipal Party Headquarters stood at the entrance, and all participating representatives had to have their letters verified. All tourists to the People's Education Center were refused entry.

Order

(1) All stand at attention, (2) Play music (Municipal Public Security Bureau Military Band), (3) Sing the Party Song, (4) Bow three times to the Party and National Flags, the President's portrait, and the portrait of Confucius, (5) The chairman respectfully reads the President's will, (6) Sacrifice to Confucius and present flowers, (7) Chairman's report, (8) Speech, (9) Sing the Confucius Commemorative Song, (10) Play music and dismiss the meeting.

Staff

The presidium of the meeting was composed of Wu Tiecheng (represented by Pan Gongzhan) of the Municipal Government, Tong Xingbai of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Yang Xiaotian of the Security Office, Yu Zhenhui of the Municipal Farmers' Association, Ye Xianggao of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, Huang Zaoxiong of the Municipal Education Association, and Wang Dasui of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. The master of ceremonies was Peng Quji, the recorder was Du Mengsen, and the director of reception was Li Dachao. There were also ushers and security guards such as Zhang Yuliang. All were on duty at the site.

Presenting Flowers

After the ceremony was conducted as scheduled, Chairman Pan Gongzhan first performed the ritual of sacrificing to Confucius and presenting flowers. Pan walked to the incense table, bowed once to the portrait of Confucius, then respectfully presented a bouquet of flowers with both hands, bowed again to the portrait of Confucius, inserted the flowers into the vase, and retreated with three bows. At that time, the Datong Orchestra played music three times and ended.

Report

After the Confucius worship ceremony, Chairman Pan Gongzhan gave a report, briefly stating that he was representing Mayor Wu in reporting the significance of commemorating Confucius. The Central Government designated August 27th as the Confucius Birthday Commemoration Day last year, and it has been held every year since. Now that the Chinese nation is on the verge of crisis, it is essential to promote China's inherent morality. China has a history of more than 4,000 years, and there are many sages worthy of respect and worship, but Confucius is the most important. Confucius was the greatest sage in Chinese history who carried on the past and opened up the future. Confucius was born in the Spring and Autumn Period. At that time, Chinese scholarship and civilization were very developed, and Confucius inherited all the sacred ways of the past and inspired all the scholarship and morality of the future. Confucius was a sage of his time. The so-called time means continuous flow, and it is all-encompassing and all-inclusive. Therefore, his learning was profound and his morality was noble, truly worthy of worship and respect for all generations. Today, China's inherent morality has been in decline for a long time, causing the national spirit to slump. Therefore, in order to save it, Confucius' morality and scholarship should be re-emphasized and promoted.

(Photo by Qichang)

Speech

After the Chairman's report, Tong Xingbai gave a speech, briefly stating that Confucius was a great sage revered by all generations in China. Now the National Government has designated August 27th as the nationally designated Confucius Birthday Commemoration Day because Confucius' morality and scholarship are truly worthy of worship by all ages. Due to the environmental factors of the time, some of the doctrines created by Confucius may not be in line with today's trends, but we should know that material things can be improved, doctrines can be changed, but truth is eternal. The truth that Confucius revealed to us, even for thousands of years, should not be denied by anyone, and should be followed by us for all generations. Confucius is the foundation of the Chinese nation's spirit, so in order to promote China's inherent national spirit, we should strive to promote Confucius' scholarship and morality. After Tong's speech, the Confucius Commemorative Song was sung, music was played, and the meeting was dismissed.

The Shanghai County Government convened all county government staff yesterday to hold a commemorative meeting in the government auditorium to mark the Confucius Birthday Commemoration on the 27th of this month. More than 100 people attended. County Magistrate Ye Zhendong presided over the meeting. First, the Chairman reported the significance of the commemoration, and then the County Education Bureau Director Zhu Changlin and others gave speeches on Confucius' scholarship and morality. The meeting then adjourned. In addition, all prosperous towns such as Minhang, Zhuanqiao, Beiqiao, Maqiao, Sanlin, and Chenhang in Pudong West and other counties of the county also raised flags to celebrate and held separate commemorative meetings.

According to the Shenshi News Agency, Ding Guitang, a specialist dispatched by the Ministry of Finance to Europe and America to inspect customs administration and the Taxation Secretary of the General Affairs Section of the former General Customs Office, set sail this spring in March. Ding Guitang (in the center) with those who welcomed him (photographed by Zhu Shunlin)

It is Reported that Fu Rulin Returned to Beijing Yesterday - Fundamental Measures for Flood Control 102

Fu Rulin, Chairman of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, came to Shanghai this time to pay his respects to Finance Minister Kong and Hubei Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Qun to discuss disaster relief for the Yangtze River floods. He has completed his official duties and took the Shanghai-Beiping train back to Beijing yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. A Central News Agency reporter met Mr. Fu at the station yesterday and inquired about the future progress of water conservancy and disaster relief for the Yangtze River. According to him, he first went to Avenue Seehaye this morning (i.e., yesterday morning) to pay his respects to Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi to discuss disaster relief funds. Then, he visited Zhang Qun, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, on Avenue Albert, to discuss the Yangtze River water conservancy and disaster relief issues in Hubei Province, and considerable results have been achieved. The Yangtze River flood this time affected a wide area, and there are many disaster victims awaiting relief. The Hubei Provincial Government has requested a disaster relief fund of 5 million yuan from the Central Government. How to raise this amount is still under discussion. It is expected that the Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Railways will provide considerable assistance. Other fundraising methods are still under consideration. Only after the urgent relief matters are resolved can we talk about agricultural and industrial relief. As for the future progress of water conservancy for the Yangtze River, it is still under active research. In recent years, the Yangtze River has flooded almost every flood season, causing frequent floods of various sizes. Therefore, the water conservancy problem can no longer be delayed. Raising the river dikes to prevent overflow is a temporary emergency measure and not a fundamental solution. Nie Yufu, the water conservancy expert from the League of Nations who was previously invited, came to China to inspect the Yangtze River and Yellow River water conservancy and believed that raising the dike body year by year was not a long-term solution and could lead to endless troubles. The fundamental solution for water management is to dredge the waterways on the one hand and to excavate tributaries on both sides of the river on the other. He greatly agrees with Mr. Nie's proposal and believes that dredging the waterways is the only essential step in water management. How to proceed is currently under research and discussion. As for the fundamental disaster relief measures proposed by Xu Shiying, Chairman of the Relief Commission, they are also under study.

What is the current situation like? Please send a telegram to inform me at any time. If there is an urgent need for relief, I will do my best to appeal and raise funds to assist in benevolent governance. Your younger brother, Xu Shiying, bows."

The Xihu Long-Distance Bus Company Will Reduce Fares Next Month - In Addition to the Original 20% Discount, Another 20% Discount Will Be Applied 106

According to Dagong News Agency, since the Xihu Long-Distance Bus Company started operating on the 17th of this month, it has been quite crowded with passengers. The company is now offering an additional 20% discount on top of the existing 20% discount on fares, starting from September 1st, to ease the burden on passengers, due to rural bankruptcy and economic difficulties for people in the interior. A reporter from Dagong News Agency obtained the following details from the company yesterday:

Business Overview Since the opening of the Xihu Bus Company on the 17th of this month, it has been ten days until yesterday. The company's full-line operations have sold an average of approximately 1,500 yuan in tickets. Among them, the Shanghai-Changshu, Wuxi-Changshu, Suzhou-Changshu, Shanghai-Taicang, and Jiading routes are more crowded with passengers. Currently, the Xihu Road has been slightly damaged due to the large number of vehicles traveling on the opening day. The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department's Highway Administration has ordered repairs to be completed, and the vehicles currently traveling on it are extremely stable.

Company Announcement The company originally planned to sell tickets for 3 cents per kilometer. During the opening period, a 20% discount was generally offered to show preferential treatment. Recently, in light of commercial depression and rural bankruptcy, and to reduce the burden on passengers, it has been decided to offer another 20% discount on fares starting from September 1st. The company issued an announcement stating: "Rural areas are bankrupt, affecting cities. At this time of autumn harvest, our company, in consideration of the economic situation of the masses, will specially reduce all ticket prices starting from September 1st to ease the burden and benefit the people. This is a special announcement."

Reduced Fares Starting from September 1st, the company will reduce all fares on all lines by 20% across the board, on top of the previously stipulated 20% discount. Therefore, the average fare is only slightly less than 2 cents per kilometer. The following is an excerpt of the reduced fares for important towns: (2) Shanghai to Nanxiang is 3 dimes, to Jiading is 5 dimes and 6 cents, to Taicang is 9 dimes, to Changshu is 1 yuan and 7 dimes, to Wuxi is 2 yuan and 6 dimes, Suzhou to Changshu is 7 dimes. All other small stations will be discounted by 20% from the original price. It is also learned that the Hutai Long-Distance Bus Company is also planning to further reduce fares for tickets from Shanghai to Jiading and Luodian next month to ease the burden on passengers.

The coffin of the late martyr Liao Zhongkai, after being transferred from Guangzhou to Shanghai and then to Beijing last month, has been temporarily placed in Linggu Temple. The Canadian Trade Commissioner to China, Scott, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday - Will Go to Beijing to Meet Minister Chen to Discuss Promoting Trade Between China and Canada 109

The newly appointed Canadian Trade Commissioner to China, Mr. Scott, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 11:00 AM aboard the Empress of Japan to succeed the previous Commissioner Cosgrave. Mr. Scott is a key member of the Canadian Department of Commerce. During the European War, he served in the Royal Air Force of Great Britain. Later, he entered Queen's University to specialize in economics. He then joined the Department of Agriculture, followed by the Department of Commerce. He also served as the Trade Commissioner of Canada in Liverpool. In 1931, he was transferred back to participate in the Ottawa British Empire Economic Conference and served as a tax advisor for the country. Later, he was transferred to Argentina as a Trade Commissioner. Now he has been transferred to China. After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Scott will go to Beijing to meet with Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry, to discuss promoting trade between China and Canada.

Vietnam

Newly Produced Domestic Lithopone Powder is Selling Well 123

Lithopone powder, commonly known as zinc sulfide, is essential for the glass industry and rubber factory printing. Our country is unable to manufacture it, and more than ten million yuan is imported every year. The huge loss is shocking. Now, Mr. Gao Enhong, the former Minister of Communications, has established the Dongya Pigment Factory, specializing in the manufacture of lithopone powder. The factory is located in Hengyi Xili, Tianbao Road, Zhabei, and the office is located at No. 8, Tailai Lane, Maigen Road, in the British Concession. It has now been produced. After being tested by the Ministry of Industry, the quality is excellent and better than imported products. Merchants are vying to buy and try it out, and they all say it is cheap and of good quality. Sales are increasing day by day, which is truly a way to recover rights and reduce the loss.
