The Two Railways Curtail Spending; Regulations on Personnel and Construction Restrictions

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Administrations, in order to strictly curtail spending and alleviate economic difficulties in accordance with orders, have stipulated six restrictions on personnel and four strict restrictions on all construction projects of the Engineering Department. Instructions have been issued to comply accordingly. Personnel: (1) If there are vacancies in the staff of each section, segment, station, or office, efforts should be made to allocate existing staff. If it is absolutely impossible to allocate them, no replacements will be assigned for the time being. (2) The monthly fixed travel expenses for nine clerks, including Shen Qiufang, in each section will be changed to seven yuan each. (3) Attendees of section affairs meetings will be paid one yuan per day for meal expenses and will not be allowed to claim travel expenses. (4) The monthly fixed travel expenses for weighbridge mechanics and workers will be changed to five yuan each. (5) When regular employees are temporarily assigned to substitute work, all travel expenses should be calculated according to the current substitute travel expenses (i.e., calculated at seven yuan, five yuan, and three yuan per month) and paid in the salary list. (6) If employees on trains are temporarily transferred to serve in sections or stations and the date reaches ten days or more, they should be reported, and their original travel expenses should be deducted. (The above will be implemented from September 1st). Construction: (1) The current method of receiving materials should be temporarily suspended. (2) In the future, the Engineering Department will cut off the basis for the original establishment of the sections and segments. From now on, this function will no longer be used. (3) The number of artisans and small workers in the Engineering Department and its affiliated factories shall be determined by the Engineering Department. In the following six months, the engineers of each section can only repair what is deemed necessary, and will not make furniture or carry out useless improvements. If there are places that need to be repaired in each office, they should first consult with the Engineering Department, and then the department will instruct the engineers of each section to handle it. (4) All places and offices, or if there are new plans, should be strictly investigated for any savings that can be made, and what cannot be saved and is truly needed should be determined. Do not make any changes in the middle.

Seeking Missing Boy Yu Dingguo 125

Yu Dingguo, from Jinshan, Jiangsu, is seventeen years old. He was studying at the Sino-French Institute of Technology. Currently, his sister is going out to find people to inquire and search. If he encounters an accident on the way, it is hoped that someone will send a message to inform him so that he can be rescued, and his sister's heart can be at ease. Stolen Xiang Sheng Motor Car Used; Found on Sanjiao Street, Shanghai Military Camp 131

Yesterday (27th), at about 1:40 a.m., the Xiang Sheng Motor Car Company on Beijing Road suddenly received a call requesting to hire a car and asking it to drive to the entrance of the Southeast Hotel on Baker Road to wait. The accounting office of the company sent driver Zhang Awu to drive the car with concession license number 18426 and Chinese license number 4826 to the front of the hotel. A bandit wearing a white short shirt and pants jumped into the car and asked the driver to drive to Zhongshan Road in West Shanghai. Zhang immediately drove west. At the intersection of Carter Road, four more bandits jumped into the car. When the car reached Zhongshan Road, the man asked to go west again and stopped near the Huafeng Printing Press on Lincoln Road. Two bandits jumped down, pulled out handguns, dragged the driver down, and said, "Help, help." The car was driven away quickly by three bandits. The driver's five yuan in cash and dozens of small coins were searched and stolen, and he was ordered to stand on the roadside and not move. After about ten minutes, the two bandits also ran away quickly. The driver shouted for help, and Cui Shulin, a volunteer policeman from the Huafeng Printing Press, drove the police car to the scene and sent the driver to the Zhoujiaqiao substation to report the incident, which was relayed to the Caojiadu branch. Wei Patrol Officer, together with detectives Wang Yixin and Su Ruiting, searched for the bandits to no avail. At dawn, at about 5 a.m., the car was found on Sanjiao Street in the Shanghai Military Camp in the South City. The police officers from the Ximen branch found the car, and the company went to retrieve it.

House Collapse on Tibet Road Yesterday Morning Results in Tragedy; Old Balcony Unable to Withstand Wind and Rain; Sudden Collapse Injures Two Men and Women 133

Heavy rain fell again at 2 a.m. yesterday, and stopped after about half an hour. At about 3 a.m., heavy rain continued to fall, and the rain was torrential. All the roads were flooded due to the inability to drain the water. At 0:10 p.m., floating clouds passed the sun, and it rained again for a moment. After the rain, the sunshine was sometimes hidden and sometimes visible, and the heat and humidity did not abate.

Buildings Along the Street

The Zhu Yisheng Cotton Shop at No. 563 Tibet Road is a single-bay building along the road. The shop owner's wife, Zhu Zhang, is from Longhua and is 43 years old. The shop is operated jointly by her eldest son, Jin Gui (22 years old), her second son, Sheng Gen (14 years old), and her husband's elder brother, Zhu Defa (53 years old).

Sudden Collapse

In addition to the shop downstairs facing the street, the kitchen behind it is used as a bedroom. The upper floor is rented out to others. Above the kitchen is the balcony of the upper floor. The building is old. At 4:30 a.m. yesterday, after the heavy rain, the balcony of the house, unable to withstand the heavy rain, suddenly collapsed with a great force. The kitchen below immediately collapsed.

Two People Injured

At that time, tiles, wood, and stones flew in all directions. Zhu Zhang, the wife of the Zhu Yisheng Cotton Shop who was staying in the kitchen, and her husband's elder brother, Zhu Defa, were both buried in the rubble. Fortunately, her two sons escaped. Her two sons invited neighbors to open the rubble and timber and rescue the two. They had all been slightly or seriously injured. Zhu Zhang was injured in the head and internal organs, and her injuries were serious. Zhu Defa was injured in the legs, etc., and his injuries were less serious.

Neighbor Affected

At the same time, the balcony of Zhao Chengshan's catering shop at No. 561 on the right was also partially collapsed by the earthquake, but the loss was minimal. After the incident, the fire department was reported by telephone, and a rescue vehicle was dispatched. Zhu Defa and Zhu Zhang were taken to Renji Hospital for treatment. The fire department also sent personnel to search in the rubble to see if there were any more injured people. When the Datong News Agency reporter went to investigate again yesterday evening, Zhu Defa had already been sent back by car after being bandaged because his injuries were less serious, but Zhu Zhang had not yet escaped danger.

Japanese Police Officer Learns to Drive a Car, Runs Over and Kills a Child 134

The family is unwilling to collect the body; it is collected by the Pushan Cemetery

A Japanese police officer at the Yulin Road Police Station No. 218, at about 2 p.m. on the 25th of this month, was learning to drive a cargo truck No. 16916 on Andong Road from south to north. The driver of the car, Chen Ar-er (from Yangzhou, residing at No. 4661, Robertson Road), sat beside him to instruct him on driving skills. Unexpectedly, several coolie children living nearby were playing there, seeing that the car was not moving very fast, they gathered around it and walked around it for fun. Among them was Huang Anzhong's son, named Daxi, who was only twelve years old. He tried to grab the iron bar on the side of the car, but his hand slipped and he fell to the ground immediately. He was crushed by the rear wheel of the car and was seriously injured. The Japanese police officer knew about it and quickly applied the brakes, but it was too late. The Yulin Road Police Station was notified, and an ambulance was called to rush the child to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died soon after. Chinese and Western detectives went to investigate. They carried the child's body to the Feilun Road autopsy office. Yesterday morning, they reported to the First Special District Local Court, which appointed Prosecutor Tang, together with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, etc., to come to the office to examine the body. First, the Western police chief informed him of the previous situation and said that the driver of the car, Chen Ar-er, had been sent to the First Special Court for custody, so that an investigation could be carried out. According to the witness Feng Suohai, a 19-year-old peddler from Nantong, he was passing by the area that day and saw the deceased hanging on the iron bar of the car when the car was turning, and then fell to the ground and was crushed by the car. According to the Japanese police officer No. 218, named Neng Qi Yu, 24 years old, residing at No. 227 Huasheng Road, he did not have a driver's license and did not know how to drive. On that day, the driver agreed to instruct me on the side, but I did not see the deceased hanging on the side of the car, slipping and falling to the ground and being crushed by the car. According to the corpse's father, Huang Anzhong, who lives in a straw shed with no number on Longjiang Road and makes a living by working, he only knew that the deceased went out to buy things that day, and did not know that he was crushed by a car, so he asked for justice. Tang Jun believed that the police had not found any fault with the driver of the car, etc., and did not file a public prosecution. The Japanese police officer and the driver Chen Ar-er were willing to contribute to the cost of the coffin because the family of the deceased was poor, but the corpse's father did not want to accept it and refused to collect the body. Tang Jun then issued an order that the deceased Huang Daxi, male, was indeed crushed to death by a 16916 truck before his death. The deceased's father, Huang Anzhong, came to the scene and claimed that he did not want to collect the body. The body was handed over to the Pushan Cemetery for collection.

Private Shipping Companies Implement Steward Reform 135

Following the China Merchants Bureau to Vigorously Implement the New Movement; Those Found Demanding Tips for Liquor are Immediately Dismissed

Since the Nanchang New Life Movement General Association ordered all shipping companies to implement New Life training and vigorously carry out reforms, in addition to the state-owned China Merchants Bureau, which has already started training stewards, other private companies are also actively carrying out reforms. A reporter from the Central News Agency explored the situation from the Shipping Association as follows:

Post Slogans; Ban Liquor Tips

The implementation of the New Life Movement by private shipping companies dates back to April this year. At that time, the Public Security Bureau and the authorities of each company selected important slogans from the New Movement and posted them everywhere in the South City to arouse the attention of stewards and passengers. Recently, the shipping companies, in view of the convenience felt by passengers after the China Merchants Bureau's Xinjiangtianyu was reformed, are now trying to ban liquor tips in order to compete.

Cold Water Stewards Automatically Disappear

The shipping companies that have implemented the ban on liquor tips include Ningxin, Xin Ningshao, Xin Hongxing, etc. The company authorities stipulate that if a steward still demands tips for liquor, he will be immediately dismissed upon discovery. This system is very effective. In the future, cold water class stewards will have no profit to make after this system is implemented and will inevitably disappear. Recently, Yan Baohang, secretary of the New Life Movement General Association, went to the Shipping Association to explain everything. The association expressed its strong approval and will follow the China Merchants Bureau to work hard to carry out the reforms.

Steward Training Postponed

The training of stewards is temporarily not implemented because private companies have many difficulties. However, if the China Merchants Bureau's results are satisfactory in the future, they will also follow suit. The ban on liquor tips can also be implemented in the Yangtze River basin in the near future. In the future, stewards who are not registered with the company authorities will be strictly prohibited from boarding the ship. In this way, it will not only vigorously promote the New Movement, but also provide great convenience to passengers.

Picking Jujubes, Striking and Killing Cousin 138

Han Jinshan Dies Unjustly, Han Guomou Flees Overnight

Han Jinshan (38 years old), a villager from Hankai Village, Hedong, Cherry Township, about six li east of Minhang Town in the southwest of this county, was washing doors and windows by a small river next to the threshing ground in front of his house at around 10 AM the day before yesterday (25th). At that time, his cousin Han Guomou (29 years old) was climbing a white jujube tree on the house foundation's threshing ground to pick white jujubes (Note: There are four jujube trees planted on the threshing ground, jointly owned by the Han clan). Han Jinshan saw this and, believing that the white jujubes were not yet ripe, shouted to stop him. Han Guomou, hearing the sound, became angry out of embarrassment and immediately climbed down the tree. Without asking why, he punched Han Jinshan. Unexpectedly, the blow struck a vital point, and Han Jinshan fell to the ground, unable to get up. Clan members, hearing the sound, came out to mediate and helped Han Jinshan back to his house, where he lay on the bed, groaning incessantly. Before an hour had passed, a tragic cry was heard, and he died. The murderer, Han Guomou, fled into the night without a trace. Clan members gathered to report to the authorities for an inquest. However, because the deceased's wife, Han Wang, had rushed back to her mother's house in Zhudi Town before the incident, there was no one to handle the matter. Therefore, someone was sent to urge Han Wang to return home to take charge. Thus, it was not until yesterday afternoon that Hu Jingmei, the head of the 21st Bao 7th Tu, and the deceased's brother, Han Runshu, reported to the local court to request an inquest. Magistrate Lei Binzhang of the Inspection Office summoned the case and, after questioning, instructed the Bao to wait at the scene of the death, awaiting the inquest.

Cao Dexin, the owner of Hehua Cigarette Paper Store at No. 159, Longhua Road, Nanshi, was opening his shop at 5:30 AM yesterday morning when three robbers suddenly arrived. One robber was wearing a blue cloth shirt, and two were wearing white cloth shirts. Speaking with an out-of-town accent, they broke into the shop and robbed 1,800 copper coins from the counter. At that time, Tang Yaocuan, a 16-year-old apprentice from Changzhou, was returning from fetching water outside when he saw the robbers robbing and shouted for help. Unexpectedly, one of the robbers wearing a white cloth shirt shot him twice, hitting him in the head, and he immediately fell to the ground and died. Seeing that they had caused a disaster, the robbers scattered and fled with the stolen goods. Branch Chief Li ordered Detective Squad Leader Shen Wenda and Detective Liu Wenhui to go to the scene for investigation. Yesterday afternoon at 1 PM, the court sent a prosecutor to the scene for an inquest. He confirmed that the death was caused by a gunshot wound to the head. In addition to completing the death certificate and ordering the arrest of the fleeing robbers to be brought to justice, he also ordered the shop owner to prepare a coffin for burial.

Love at First Sight at a Wedding Banquet: Man and Woman Cohabit Privately 140

Huang Liansheng Accused of Interfering with Marriage, Lu Zhenying Claims She Was Deceived and Imprisoned

Lu Bingsheng, a tailor from Pudong at No. 1126, Dongyouheng Road, has a daughter named Zhenying, 29 years old and somewhat attractive. On October 14 two years ago, at a wedding banquet at the home of his relative Zhu Agen, she met Huang Yunsheng, a fellow villager from Chuansha. They fell in love at first sight. In January of the following year, Huang took advantage of an opportunity to take the woman to the Pingqiao Hotel on Xizang Road, where they rented a room and slept together. The woman's father was completely unaware. At that time, Huang was learning how to make new-style suitcases in Cangji Street, Nanshi. Recently, he lost his job and went to Lu's house, saying that the woman's tailoring business had very little profit, and it would be better to cooperate with him in the suitcase business, which could yield a large profit. Lu happily agreed and abandoned his old business to learn this kind of work. From then on, Huang stayed at their house and secretly engaged in illicit affairs with the woman. However, the new-style small suitcases they made could not be sold on the market and no one asked about them. Their capital was stranded, and Huang secretly borrowed clothes and farm implements from the woman. Unable to gain a foothold, at around 7 AM on the 17th of this month, he tricked the woman into going to his house in Chuansha, Pudong, where they lived as husband and wife. After his daughter disappeared, Lu Bingsheng learned that Huang Liansheng had abducted her and that they were living together in Chuansha. The day before yesterday, Bingsheng went to the place where Huang's parents agreed to bring Liansheng and Zhenying home for a discussion, and a big quarrel ensued. Chinese police officer and detective Huang Fugen from No. 2039 inquired about the whole story. Lu Bingsheng then brought Huang Liansheng to the Huishan Police Station for overnight detention. The next morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer at the Bureau of Works, explained the previous situation and filed a public prosecution in accordance with Article 241, Section 3 of the Criminal Law, for the crime of interfering with marriage and family. Subsequently, Lu Bingsheng claimed that his daughter had been promised to someone else and could not marry the defendant. The woman, Zhenying, said that she had asked the defendant for three pieces of clothing that had been pawned that morning. He said that he had to go to his home in Chuansha to return them in full, and she was deceived. Afterwards, she was imprisoned in a room and not allowed to go outside. When questioned, the defendant claimed that the woman had followed him back to his hometown voluntarily. He was evasive about the rest and asked for leniency. Judge Jiang Shuzi ruled that he would remain in custody pending sentencing.

Two Children Scalded to Death by Hot Water 141

Ma Wenhua, a 34-year-old sock merchant from Nanxiang, lives in his hometown. His wife, Zhu, from Shaoxing, had four children, but only one son, Ma Dejian, survived. When their third child died, Zhu became even more resentful and unhappy all day long, which was evident on her face. Her husband took her and his son, Dejian, to Shanghai to live in his mother-in-law's house at No. 8, Xingyi Lane, No. 545, Kangnuot Road, in order to relieve her depression. However, at around 9 AM on the 21st of this month, Dejian was playing in the living room when he accidentally knocked over a kettle of boiling water placed on the floor. At that time, the child's aunt, Zhu Yunmei, who was holding her two-year-old son, Zhu Yun, was also having breakfast there. Seeing this, she rushed to rescue them, but due to panic, she slipped and fell to the ground. As a result, both the woman and the child were scalded by the boiling water. After being seen by family members, the two children were immediately sent to Baolong Hospital for treatment. Yunmei suffered only minor injuries to her legs at the time, so she was not sent to the hospital. However, one of the children died because of their severe injuries, which could not be saved. The hospital reported to the Gordon Road Police Station, which ordered detective Gao Huixian to investigate. The two corpses were taken to the Feilun Road Morgue on the previous two days. Chen Shandong, the head of the Chinese police at the police station, reported to the First Special District Local Court, which dispatched prosecutors Guo and Tang to the morgue to confirm that the two children had died from being scalded by boiling water. They then ordered the families of the deceased to sign statements and take the bodies back for burial.

(2) Do not reduce wages. (3) Do not dismiss workers without reason. The Railway Bureau has given it consideration. Railway Bureau News

There are no so-called new workers. The incompatibility between the cooperative and the temporary workers has a long history. In recent months, there have been more than 20 fights, which have not only hurt both workers but also affected cargo transportation, causing complaints from merchants. The Traffic Office of the Railway Bureau, in order to maintain cargo transportation, has submitted a request to appoint Sun Zhu to be responsible for the reorganization. The cause of the incident the day before yesterday was that cooperative workers and temporary workers met on Jiaotong Road and, because of their old grudges, attacked each other. More and more people gathered, leading to a tragic incident in which both sides were injured. However, reports that a certain worker was beaten to death are completely false rumors deliberately spread by a certain party.

Memorial to Layman Wu Jichen, Supporter of the Song Tripitaka 143

The Song Tripitaka, printed by the Shanghai Song Edition Tripitaka Association, has been published to 550 volumes and will soon be completed. It was initially initiated by Zhu Ziqiao, Ye Yufu, Wu Jichen, and others, who worked hard and went through great difficulties. Wu Jichen, in particular, was brave and diligent in promoting and distributing the Tripitaka. He passed away on the 20th of this month due to illness. In his dying wish, he requested that a copy of the Tripitaka be purchased and donated to Chao'an Temple in Zhenjiang for eternal offering. His lifelong devotion is unparalleled and in harmony with the Buddha's light. Zhu and Ye have specially written a memorial poem and a mourning couplet to express their sorrow and admiration. The memorial words for Layman Wu Jichen are as follows:

"The public's faith in the Buddha, is unwavering; The Buddha's embrace of the public, endures for countless kalpas. This association, is a model for our followers; Wishing to help it reach completion, why not wait a moment? Considering the public's sincerity, how can ink and paper fully depict it? May this Tripitaka be protected without end, and may the surname be engraved forever in the Qisha district."

The couplet reads:

"Protecting the golden scripture through many battles, this wish is about to be fulfilled, the kalpa is fleeting, the public cannot wait; A building is completed as a pure land, rebirth is easy, anxieties and worries fill the world, how can it be endured."

Imported at 2 PM, Berthing at Shun Tai Wharf, After Sailing to Qingdao at the End of the Month and Returning to Shanghai, Offering Visits

Jardine Matheson's new ship Desheng, sailing on the South China line, is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai this afternoon at 2 PM from the UK on its maiden voyage and berth at the Shun Tai Wharf in Hongkou. After sailing to Qingdao at the end of the month and returning to Shanghai, visits will be arranged in due course. The details are recorded as follows:

Arriving in Shanghai This Afternoon

Jardine Matheson, in order to compete with China Merchants on the South China route, specially built a new ship, the Desheng, in the UK. The ship is 325 feet long, 48 feet wide, and 27 feet deep, with a net weight of over 4,000 tons. It travels at 16 nautical miles per hour and uses the latest engines and machinery. It has 13 first-class cabins, more than 100 steerage seats, six suites, and more than ten large dining rooms. The decoration is luxurious, with escorts and sanitary equipment. It is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai this afternoon at 2 PM from the UK on its maiden voyage and berth at the Shun Tai Wharf in Hongkou.

Sailing to Qingdao at the End of the Month

This is the first time the ship has arrived in Shanghai. Jardine Matheson will allow all sectors to understand the ship's structure, equipment, and luxury. After taking passengers to Qingdao on the 31st and returning to Shanghai, visits will be arranged in due course, with tea and snacks provided. Chinese and Western staff from the company, as well as the captain, will personally host the event. It is said that the ship can return to Shanghai from Qingdao on the 4th or 5th of next month.

Radio Broadcasting Industry Flood Relief Propaganda Group's First Meeting 147

The Flood Relief Propaganda Group of the Radio Broadcasting Industry Association convened its first meeting from 2 PM to 3 PM on August 24 at the association's office on Jiangxi Road to discuss implementation methods. Committee members Lin Huayan, Zhang Yuanxian, Chen Yanggan, and Zhou Bangjun were present. Zhou Bangjun was publicly elected as chairman and Zhang Yuanxian as recorder. After performing the formalities, the purpose of the meeting was announced and the following proposals were discussed: (1) For the convenience and needs of the Propaganda Group, the Executive Committee should set up an advertising group or increase the number of committee members. (Resolution) The Executive Committee will decide. (2) Prepare to publish a special edition and solicit advertisements, with advertising revenue also used for flood relief. (Resolution) Passed. (3) First, draft the preparation organization process and distribute it to major and minor newspapers and radio stations for disclosure. (Resolution) Zhang Yuanxian will draft it and Zhou Bangjun will be responsible for handling it. (4) All regular and wrapper paper printed by member radio stations should be stamped with propaganda slogans to facilitate donations. (Resolution) Approved in principle, and the Executive Committee is requested to send a public letter to all radio stations, requesting that propaganda slogans be added to the printed materials of the merchants who broadcast advertisements. The meeting adjourned.

Second Special District Court Lawyer's Lounge Expansion Investigated 150

The Shanghai Bar Association submitted a document to the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court yesterday, requesting the expansion of the lawyer's lounge. Most of the members of the association claimed that the lawyer's lounge set up by the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court was too small. When members came to court to appear in court, they often had nowhere to rest and had to wait outside. This was both unsightly and inconvenient and should be expanded. It was proposed that the outdoor corridor, that is, the area at the bottom of the escalator, was usually unused, and it would be appropriate to use it to expand the lawyer's rest room. It would not affect the use of the original land of the court, and a proposal was submitted to the court for expansion. The situation described by the members is indeed the fact and should be expanded. We hereby request your court to allow the use of the outdoor corridor for the expansion of the lawyer's rest. As for the cost, it should be borne by the association. It should be submitted to your court for review and approval, which would be in the public interest.

Zheng Baolin's Case of Pimping His Mistress into Prostitution: Interrogation Concluded 151

Zheng Baolin, also known as Caixi, a 24-year-old man from Jiangbei, living at No. 24, Nande Shunli, Runni Ferry, Peidong, had an affair with Chen Renzhen, a 22-year-old woman from Yangzhou. Being unable to support her, he discussed the matter with the woman and obtained her consent to pawn her into prostitution at the Cantonese brothel run by Zhao Changrong (20 years old this year) at No. 1 Hemingli, Weier Meng Road, French Concession, for a price of 200 yuan, with a term of one and a half years. Half a year has passed since she was pawned. However, driven by lust, Zheng would often summon the woman to go out and meet in hotels. This caused annoyance to the madam and others, leading to disagreements. On the 17th of this month, at around 10 p.m., Zheng was suddenly attacked by several thugs wielding axes in Yu's residence, Lane 168, Huage Nie Road, French Concession, and suffered injuries to his body and legs. The assailants fled in a panic. Zheng glanced back and saw Zhao Changrong, the owner of the brothel, standing nearby. Suspecting Zhao of instigating the attack, Zheng dragged Zhao to the police station. The injured Zheng was sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment. During the interrogation, Zhao confessed that the attack was carried out by Sun Zhilan (from Xiaogaoyou, residing at No. 32, Jingyi Lane, Malang Road) and Huang Zhangda (from Wuxi, residing at No. 44, Songshan Road). The detectives then arrested Sun and Huang. They further confessed that Li Xiaoma, Xiaochangjiao, and Erheitan, who are still at large, were also involved in the assault. The victim denied their involvement in the assault. The next day, the police transferred Zhao, Sun, and Huang to the Special First Court for interrogation and investigation. Details of the case have been reported in this newspaper. The day before yesterday morning, Chen Pusheng from the Special Second Court of Shanghai presided over the continued interrogation in the Eighth Criminal Court. Yao Zhaodi, a lawyer from the Police Department, presented the case and prosecuted them for the crime of injury. Zheng Baolin, the victim, then testified about the incident and claimed that he saw Zhao Changrong standing opposite him and directing the attack. Zhao denied the accusation and hired lawyer Li Ming to defend him, presenting evidence to prove that the defendant did not participate in or instigate the assault on the plaintiff. Sun and Huang continued to testify as before. The court announced the conclusion of the interrogation and awaited a scheduled sentencing. Zhao was released on a 200 yuan shop guarantee, while the others were remanded in custody.

Wang Cao, a 51-year-old woman from Yixing, has a daughter named Wang Hongmei, who is 17 years old and of decent appearance. Unexpectedly, her mother, Wang Cao, who was urgently seeking her daughter because Hongmei had been betrothed to a man named Chen from the same village, happened to meet her on the road. Rice Shop Employee Commits Suicide After Losing His Job 153

Gu Hongsheng, a 30-year-old man from Liuhe, had been working at the Yongyi Rice Shop on Sanyang Road in Zhabei. Recently, he was dismissed by the shop manager due to negligence. Gu became distraught and conceived the idea of ending his life. On the 24th, at 2 p.m., he went alone to the Southeast Hotel at No. 11 opposite Ruifu Lane, West Zilaihuo Street, French Concession, and registered as Gu Hongnan, renting room 46 upstairs. That night, he went out and bought raw opium to commit suicide. He had previously sent a letter to his younger brother, Gu Sanbao (23 years old, working at the Yongji Rice Shop at No. 542, Kangnao Tuo Road, Public Concession), asking to borrow some pocket money and instructing him to deliver it to the Southeast Hotel. The next day at noon, his brother brought several silver dollars to the Southeast Hotel to visit him. The tea boy, Zhou Zhiren (36 years old, from Haimen), led him upstairs and knocked on the door of room 46, calling out for a long time without response. They then found a way to open the door and entered the room. Gu was lying supine on the bed, his face pale and ashen, saliva foaming from his mouth, unable to speak, barely alive, and in critical condition. Realizing that he had taken poison, his brother immediately hired a rickshaw to take him to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, the opium poison had spread deeply in his abdomen, and the medical treatment was ineffective. He died at 5:30 p.m. on the 26th. The hospital reported to the police station, which sent detectives to investigate. Gu's body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for an autopsy. His brother was notified. As yesterday was the birthday of Confucius, the Supreme Sage and Teacher, it was a holiday. The report will be submitted to the Special Second Court today for officials to examine.

Zhou Xu, a 36-year-old woman from Jiangyin, lives in a pavilion room at No. 10, Dingxing Lane, Xingjia Po Road, West Shanghai, and works in a factory for a living. Without saying a word, he drew a sharp knife from his side and stabbed her in the waist. He then turned around and fled. Zhou woke up in pain and cried for help. Qi Lianhong, the landlord of the second room, heard the alarm and rushed in, finding Zhou lying in a pool of blood on the bed, delirious. He then reported to the Caojiadu Branch Bureau, and detectives Zhuang Dexiu and Wang Yixin joined the search for the assailant but found no trace. It is rumored that the assassination was caused by revenge from a former lover. Medical World 165

Lion Brand Panacea Loses Lawsuit The Tiger Balm balm is effective in treating diseases and is widely popular, so there are many counterfeiters seeking profit. Guo Dongliang of Shantou Ren'antang once produced a type of Lion Brand Panacea, whose trademark and packaging were completely similar to that of Yong'antang Tiger Balm. Yong'antang legally sued them in court and filed a trademark administrative lawsuit. After many years of mutual litigation, the Executive Yuan finally ruled that the plaintiff's (i.e., Guo Dongliang's) lawsuit was dismissed and Yong'antang won the final lawsuit. The case had previously been ruled by the Executive Yuan that Ren'antang Guo Dongliang's Lion Brand and packaging did indeed imitate Yong'antang Tiger Balm, and the trademark was completely revoked. Ren'antang refused to accept this and appealed to the Administrative Court, which also ruled that the plaintiff's lawsuit was dismissed.

Letter to the Editor 168

Dear Editor, I recently read the section "Clash Between New and Old Workers at North Station" in your newspaper, and I found that it deviates slightly from the facts. I would like to present the details of the incident as follows, and wish you well. Zhu San was ordered by the Railway Bureau on the 23rd of this month to take over the loading and unloading work at the North Freight Station on August 24th and be responsible for the rectification. To prevent disturbances, Zhu San did not change any of the original workers. The treatment was in complete compliance with the regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Railways. Zhu San repeatedly announced this to the workers upon arriving at the station. The workers agreed to the takeover at the time but put forward four conditions that had to be reported to the director of the Traffic Department on the 26th before they would agree to comply. Zhu San accepted this. Therefore, there were no accidents on the 24th and 25th. On the morning of the 26th, after reporting to the director of the Traffic Department, Zhu San went to the station. The station master of the freight station, Qi, summoned the worker representatives Wei Yuemeng and Hong Yun for a discussion. Unexpectedly, a martial drama suddenly broke out outside the station before they had said a few words. Fearing that it would affect the writing room, Qi closed all the doors, and Zhu San and others were spared from the disaster. It was found that Zhu San only brought eleven people to the station and did not bring a single extra person. Outside rumors that Zhu led more than a hundred new workers to the station to take over were completely untrue. This was witnessed not only by the station master of the freight station, Qi, the section chief of the police, Zhong, and the team leader of the security office, Xue, but also by the worker representatives Zhang Yuemeng and Hong Yun. As for how the beating occurred, whether it was instigated by Zhu San, and whether Zhu San was involved, the Public Security Bureau has sent the relevant people to the court. In the future, who is right and who is wrong will naturally come to light. In short, Zhu San was ordered to rectify and acted in accordance with the bureau's order. If the workers objected, they could report to the Railway Bureau. How could they lead new workers to forcibly seize the food and clothing of the original workers? Moreover, the contracting of this work is not a contracting system, and the benefits are absolutely open. Most of the workers have already understood the content. The workers who oppose it are actually a minority. Moreover, it has been found that these minority workers do not work for nothing on weekdays, which has led to repeated disputes in the past. Without their instigation, not only would this unfortunate incident not have occurred, but there would have been no need for Zhu San to rectify it. In addition to reporting the situation to the Railway Bureau for instructions, please publish this letter in the Letter to the Editor column to avoid untrue rumors. I am deeply grateful. Yours sincerely, Sun Zhu San, Contractor for Loading and Unloading Work at the North Freight Station of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, Address: No. 17, Lane 6, Ningkang Lane, North Zhejiang Road.

To the Editor: The news item published in today's news column about the clash between new and old workers at the North Station is not consistent with the facts. Our cooperative has more than 130 loading and unloading workers who have served the Railway Bureau for nearly 20 years and have done their best. The person in charge of the cooperative, Mr. Gao Ge, has also worked in the Railway Bureau for more than ten years. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, he was promoted to worker leader and was especially valued by the directors of the Railway Bureau. As a custom, if the work is busy, our cooperative hires temporary workers to help. These workers are led by Liu Chaojin. In recent years, business has been slow, and our cooperative has been unable to give the temporary workers work from time to time. Liu Chaojin has always wanted to seize the duties of our cooperative, so he is cooperating with Sun Zhu San. Sun's son, Lü Ping, claims to be a secretary somewhere and is said to be the most trusted confidant of the director. With this help, Liu has become even more rampant and unscrupulous. On the 1st of this month, he led six or seventy temporary workers to our cooperative to beat us up. He then reported the incident to the police station. Suddenly, a detective sent by the garrison headquarters came and arrested our Gao Ge and Cui Shita, and they have been detained until now. Now Sun, together with Liu and Secretary Zhao from somewhere, led more than 200 temporary workers, each armed with pistols and knives, to the two-road station early yesterday morning to forcibly seize the work, which led to the fight. This was entirely caused by Liu, Sun, Zhao, and others. It is not that our Gao Ge has no control. All the details will be reported by our cooperative to the Central Party Headquarters and the local officials, as well as the two road directors, to seek a fair judgment. The truth will soon come to light. This is the truth, and we earnestly request your editor-in-chief to correct this and publish it in the "Letter to the Editor" column. Respectfully yours, Shanghai North Station Freight Cooperative, August 27th.

Weather Report 169

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated that the Yellow Sea will be cloudy with strong northwesterly to northeasterly winds and intermittent rain. The Yangtze River Basin will be cloudy with occasional showers and strong northeasterly to northerly winds. The weather around the world and the East China Sea will be very bad, with strong cyclones and rain, due to a hurricane southeast of Dajima moving northwest-north. The small low-pressure center east of Dongsha Island may still move northeast, passing through southern Taiwan. The center of the hurricane was within 60 miles of 28 degrees north latitude and 130 degrees east longitude at 3 p.m., moving north or northwest-north, with strong winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 p.m. yesterday, the temperature in this city was a high of 91.6 and a low of 79.2. On the same day last year, the high was 98.6 and the low was 76.

Results of the Second Solicitation of Educational Film Scripts by the Jiangsu Department of Education 175

In order to promote educational films, the Jiangsu Department of Education publicly solicited educational film scripts for the first time last year. The requirements of the Jiangsu Department of Education for applicants have also progressed from only requiring a simple story to a detailed multi-act script. Therefore, the works submitted this time are mostly from the hands of experts, creating a dazzling and beautiful collection. It is said that the theme of the play is to narrate the importance of sound maternal education in influencing children's physical and mental health, and the various struggles of mothers for the sake of their children's future. The plot is tragic and impassioned, moving people's hearts. In order to strive for perfection, the Jiangsu Department of Education asked Mr. Chen Guofu to provide detailed instructions and modifications for each point. Therefore, not only is the content more perfect, but the educational significance and the dramatic expressiveness are also considered comprehensively and thoroughly.

Mr. Hu Puan's Opinion on Separate Schools for Boys and Girls: Male and Female Temperaments are Different, and Training and Education Naturally Differ Slightly; Local Customs are Different, so it is Advisable to Adapt to Local Conditions 176

Since the Beiping Municipal Government advocated separate schools for boys and girls, it has attracted the attention of people in the education circles in various places. Yesterday, a reporter from the Shanghai News Agency specially visited Mr. Hu Puan, a famous scholar of Chinese culture, to inquire about his opinion on separate schools for boys and girls. He was pleased to express his views as follows: Mr. Hu said that boys and girls must have the same knowledge, which is the educational principle of the modern world. Coeducation in our country has been implemented for a short time after the state's formulation. Recently, some provinces and cities have advocated the system of separate schools, which has not been approved by the central government, causing repercussions in schools. The reform of the education system is a major matter, and it is necessary to gather the cooperative spirit of all three parties, consider its advantages and disadvantages, and make a plan for prompt agreement. It should not be implemented in a [hasty] manner.

Discussion Among Celebrities

Now that there is freedom of speech, all celebrities who have deeply studied the boy-girl school system can publish their opinions in newspapers and magazines for the authorities to adopt. Because boys and girls have different temperaments, there are slight differences in the two key points of teaching and training. Their main courses can be studied together, and some subjects such as home economics, even in the same school, should be set up in separate elective classrooms for girls for separate teaching. In addition, girls are physically weaker, and their physical education should also pay attention to separate practice. This is a discussion of coeducation and separate education in terms of principles, but it is necessary to carefully examine the academic atmosphere of each place and each school, and to measure the advantages and disadvantages of teaching and training to determine which standard is more suitable for the coeducation system or the separate education system as a basis for choice.

Proposals from Provinces and Cities

Provincial and municipal departments and bureaus are closer to local situations and should often inspect the schools under their jurisdiction at ordinary times to understand the actual situation in detail. They should also widely collect opinions from celebrities and public opinion for reference. If there is a closed atmosphere in the area under their jurisdiction, such as in northern China, where many old families adhere to old habits and would rather girls lose their education if there are no girls' schools, then it may be permissible to make a proposal to the department for approval to establish girls' schools on a case-by-case basis. The key is to ensure that girls receive a corresponding education within the possible scope. If there are no special circumstances, the old system can be maintained.

National Formulation

Our country has difficult finances and shallow public knowledge. Coeducation for boys and girls is particularly economical. If a separate system is implemented, funding will be stretched, and there may be only a few or no girls' schools in various places, so girls will have few opportunities to attend school. Because coeducation for boys and girls is prone to abuses, the advantages and disadvantages should be weighed, and the emphasis should be placed on avoiding the serious and choosing the light to establish a system. Then the central government can have a general overview of the country's politics and education, and can adopt the trends of the opinions of famous people across the country, and submit the cases presented by various provinces and cities to the staff of the ministries and departments for special research and discussion. It is necessary to carefully consider the actual situation in various places and either continue to use the coeducation system, or change to the separate education system, or use a combination of the coeducation and separate education systems, taking the consensus of the majority, passing it at a meeting, and writing it into the regulations. It must be implemented nationwide to achieve the effect of unifying politics and education.

Zhejiang Provincial People's Education Hall Invites Yu's Chinese Typewriter for Exhibition 178

In order to promote cooperation between inventors and investors and to truly encourage the interest of Chinese people in researching science, the Zhejiang Provincial People's Education Hall has specially requested inventors across the country to select and send their products to hold a large-scale exhibition of new inventions by Chinese people on a scheduled basis. The Yu's Chinese typewriter, which was awarded Patent Certificate No. 18 by the Ministry of Industry, is related to culture. However, it has been found that senior government agencies and national postal banks almost never use it. Moreover, the structure of the machine is robust, the movement is sensitive, and it can type 20 to 30 words per minute. With carbon paper, it can type 16 to 17 copies at a time. It can also be typed on wax paper and printed with a mimeograph machine, printing hundreds or thousands of copies like a single sheet. The characters are made of steel with the hardness of copper, which greatly benefits culture. The hall believes that it is necessary to have a public exhibition and has sent a letter to Yu Binqi Chinese Typewriter Manufacturing Factory at No. 62 Zhoujia Zui Road, Shanghai, to contact them and has obtained Mr. Yu's consent to participate in the public exhibition. It is heard that other products are also being solicited, and the hall warmly welcomes all participants.

Professor Xia Chengfeng of National Central University Dies of Illness 179

Professor Xia Chengfeng (Zi Zhan Chu) of the College of Education of National Central University and former inspector of Jiangsu Province, was one of the famous professors of National Central University. He had been a professor at the school for seven years. His books, such as "Local Educational Administration" and "Education," were popular for a time and were widely circulated in domestic education circles. This time, he was invited by Hubei Province to give a lecture in Wuhan. After returning to Nanjing, he felt slightly unwell. At first, he did not pay attention, but unexpectedly, he contracted typhoid fever, and his condition became increasingly critical. He passed away on the evening of the 23rd (two days ago) at the age of only 37, leaving behind five children, the oldest of whom is only 14 years old, and parents in their 70s. The whole family usually relied solely on Mr. Xia's salary to make a living. He left nothing behind after his death, which is truly regrettable. Fortunately, he had a life insurance policy with China United Assurance Company last year through the introduction of his classmate Qian Zhisheng, but the amount is not large and is only a drop in the bucket, only enough to cover a portion of his children's education expenses. It is heard that colleagues from the College of Education of National Central University will hold a memorial service in Nanjing.

Little Boy (28) 182

— Original by Ms. Alcott of the United States, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

As Ned listened to these words, his face gradually brightened. Although his report card was not long, it had given him a great deal of spiritual encouragement, making him feel that he also had some qualifications and was not completely useless. "Yes, I can control my temper—I learned that from my father's cane; I can play the violin, although I don't know where the Tannu Tuva Sea is," he thought to himself, and there was a kind of indescribable comfort in his heart. Then he began to speak, so eagerly that Little Bridge heard him. He said:

"I really want to learn, I'm determined to do it. I never go to school, but it's not my fault; if they don't laugh at me, I guess I'll be able to do very well—you and the headmaster treat me so well."

Little Bridge forgot everything and shouted, "They're not allowed to laugh at you; if they laugh, I—I—I'll tell them they can't."

Everyone stopped their nine-by-nine-eighty-one work, and everyone looked up to see what was going on.

Mr. Pei felt that the lesson of mutual assistance was more important than arithmetic at this time, so he told them about Ned's situation, and told the story in an interesting and moving way. Therefore, these kind-hearted children agreed to give him a hand and felt honored to have been asked to share their knowledge with a talented person. This public request planted good feelings in them and reduced Ned's obstacles, because everyone was happy to give him all kinds of "tips" to help him gradually ascend the ladder of learning.

Sports News

Citywide Swimming Training to Begin on September 2; Mixed Training for One Week, Then Selection 183

The Shanghai men's and women's swimming training for this year's National Games was originally scheduled to begin on August 1 at the YMCA swimming pool on Sichuan Road, but was postponed because most of the athletes were participating in the China Youth Summer Training Camp and coach Peng Ermei had been ill for a long time, resulting in the training not being officially held. Now the organizing committee has specially changed the swimming training to start on September 2, with a week of mixed training first. The training time is from 8:00 PM to 9:00 PM every evening, and the location is the China Youth swimming pool. After one week, there will be a selection. Those who pass the selection will be official athletes representing Shanghai at this year's National Games and will continue training until the National Games open. The registration has also started at the beginning of this month. Nearly 20 people have registered with the association. Now, for the sake of popularization, the organizing committee especially allows male and female swimming athletes in this city to continue to register. Those who believe they have the following qualifications can register with the YMCA Sports Department on Sichuan Road from now until September 1, when registration will close and will not be extended. Registration is free of charge. Those who wish to show their skills at the National Games should not miss this opportunity. The qualifications are as follows:

Men

50-yard freestyle: 30 seconds, 100-yard freestyle: 1 minute 15 seconds, 100-yard backstroke: 1 minute 30 seconds, 200-yard breaststroke: 3 minutes 10 seconds, 400-yard freestyle: 6 minutes 10 seconds, 1500-yard freestyle: 24 minutes 30 seconds.

Women

50-yard freestyle: 45 seconds, 100-yard freestyle: 1 minute 50 seconds, 100-yard backstroke: 2 minutes 10 seconds, 200-yard breaststroke: 4 minutes 20 seconds.

Sixth National Games Announces Women's Outdoor Softball Rules (2) 190

Article 5: The Game

A. Right of Choice

Section 1: The right of choice between offense and defense for the two teams shall be determined by a draw.

B. Start of the Game

Section 1: The game shall begin when the umpire announces "Play." At the same time, the pitcher must throw the ball to the batter.

C. Game Time

Section 1: Number of Innings Specified: Each team should have the opportunity to bat for seven innings. However, the game may also be considered officially ended under the following circumstances: (1) If the team batting first has fewer points after the seventh inning than the team batting for only six innings; (2) If the team batting second has more points than the opposing team before the third out in the seventh inning; (3) If the umpire declares a "valid game" due to darkness or storms (see Article 5, C, Section 5).

Section 2: Minimum Number of Innings: If both team captains agree to reduce the specified number of innings, the minimum number of innings for a formal game should be four.

Section 3: Tie Game: If the two teams have the same number of points after each batting for seven innings, the game should continue until one team has more points than the opposing team in an equal number of innings. However, if the team batting second scores more points than the opposing team before the third out in any inning after the seventh, the game may end.

Section 4: Forfeiture: If a team is absent temporarily, or if it is present at the field but refuses to play within five minutes after the umpire announces "Play" at the specified time, the umpire should declare a forfeiture and determine the non-defaulting team as the winner, unless there are special circumstances causing the delay.

Section 5: Valid Game: If a game must be stopped due to darkness or storms after both teams have completed three innings, the umpire should declare a "valid game." In a declared valid game, the team with the most points in an equal number of innings is the winner, unless the team batting first has more points in fewer innings or in the last uncompleted inning than the team batting first.

Section 6: Invalid Game: If the game must be terminated due to darkness or storms and the two teams have not played a full three innings, the umpire should declare an "invalid game."

D. Determination of Game Winner and Loser

Section 1: When the umpire declares the game over (see Article 6), the team with the most points wins.

E. Game Suspension

Section 1: The umpire may declare the game "suspended" in the following circumstances: (1) When rain, darkness, or other uncontrollable situations temporarily prevent the game from proceeding. If it is still impossible to continue after a 30-minute stoppage, the umpire should declare the game over according to Sections 5 and 6 of Article 5; (2) When a player or umpire encounters an accident and cannot continue to perform their duties; (3) When a player who has been disqualified is ordered to leave the field.

Section 2: After the umpire declares "Suspension," the game is suspended until "Play" is announced to restart the game. During the suspension period, any players who are put out, advance bases, or score are invalid.

Article 6: Scoring

A runner scores one point if, before the first out, they touch each base in order and are able to return to home plate without committing any violation. However, if they reach home plate at the same time as the third forced out, or if they are put out before reaching first base, or if, even if not in conjunction, the third out occurs in that exchange, it is still invalid and no points are awarded.

Article 7: Pitching Rules

A. Legal Pitch

Section 1: Pitcher's Position: Before throwing the ball to the batter, the pitcher must have both feet on the pitching plate, facing the batter. However, when performing the throwing action, they may turn sideways to the batter. When throwing, they may take up to one step forward, and the other foot must remain in contact with the pitching plate and cannot leave it. After the ball is thrown, the pitcher may move forward towards the batter.

Section 2: Throwing Method: (1) Underhand Pitching: For 35-foot and 45-foot fields, it can be adopted at will. When throwing underhand, the arm's swing must be in the downward direction, parallel to the body. Rotating the ball is not prohibited. (2) Overhand Pitching: Overhand pitching can be freely selected on a 60-foot field. This method must be used on a 65-foot field. When throwing the ball, the arm should be from top to bottom, parallel to the ground. Rotating the ball is not prohibited.

B. Illegal Pitch

If the pitcher does not comply with the location or method of throwing, the umpire should declare an illegal pitch. "Penalty" (A) The batter is awarded one "ball"; (B) The runners can advance one base each without being put out.

C. Strikes and Balls

Section 1: Strike: A ball thrown by the pitcher without any irregularities that passes over any part of home plate, with a height above the batter's knees and below the batter's shoulders, is called a "strike." "Relationship to the Batting Team" (A) If a batter does not hit a "good" ball, it is called a "strike"; (B) The runner can advance to any base, but at the risk of being put out.

Section 2: Ball: A ball thrown by the pitcher without any irregularities, but the ball does not pass over any part of home plate, or its height is not between the batter's shoulders and knees, or the ball touches the ground before reaching home plate, is a ball unless the batter hits it.

"Penalty" (A) If a ball is not hit by the batter or does not touch the batter, the umpire should announce one "ball"; (B) The runner can advance to any base at the risk of being put out. However, when the batter becomes a runner due to four "balls" and safely advances one base, all runners originally on base must give up their base to accommodate this new runner and advance one base each without being put out (those who do not have to give up the base are not entitled to this right).

D. Dead Ball

Section 1: A ball thrown by the pitcher to the batter that touches the batter's body or clothes without being hit by the batter is called a dead ball. "Penalty" (1) If the batter is not intentionally hit by the ball: A, it should be called one "ball"; B, the runner cannot advance. However, if this ball is the fourth "ball" and the batter should become a runner and advance to first base, then the runners at each base must give way, and each advances one base without being put out. (2) If the batter deliberately lets the ball hit them: A, it should be called one "strike"; B, the runner may not advance.

E. Pitcher's Balk

Section 1: The following situations with the pitcher constitute a "pitcher's balk": (1) Having stood on the pitching plate, starting to make a pitching action, but not throwing the ball; (2) Holding the ball for too long, making an unconscious delay. "Penalties for (1) and (2)" A, it should be called one "ball"; B, all runners can safely advance one base without being put out; (3) When a runner is occupying a certain base, the pitcher makes a motion on the pitching plate to prepare to throw to that base, but does not throw; (4) The pitcher throws the ball from the pitching plate to any base, in an attempt to put the runner out, but when throwing, does not step towards that base, clearly indicating the direction of the throw. "Penalties for (3) and (4)" All runners can safely advance one base without being put out. (To be continued)

Spring and Autumn

Snippets 205

— (Yan Maode)

To be a great figure in modern times, the first thing is to train your body to be like a rattan cane - somewhat flexible, yet very strong; able to bend, yet never break; able to bow under slight pressure, yet returning to its normal uprightness and lofty spirit once the pressure is gone.

"Failure is the mother of success; success is the fruit of failure." Failure contains the seeds of success. In terms of overall evolution, failure is a low point in the long journey of evolution, a completely natural phenomenon. To be discouraged by this and lack the courage to persevere is pointless self-affliction.

The most pitiable people in the world are those who are indecisive, hesitant, and lost when faced with problems, unsure of which path to take. They are those who cannot make their own choices and only listen to others. Such people cannot gain the trust of others.

After the Engagement 206

— Lan Shan

Wearing a red gold engagement ring on the ring finger of my left hand, the heart that has been fluttering for a long time is now settling down. Although it is said to be settling down, there is still a kind of floating feeling. Thinking of the happy days to come, a burst of frivolous fluctuations arises in my heart, and a shallow smile unconsciously hangs on my face.

This is originally happiness. After wearing this ring, there is a girl in the world who belongs to you, and you yourself also belong to that girl.

Think about the past. When she had not agreed to your marriage, how uneasy were you? Afraid that she would be snatched away by others, afraid that her name could not be printed out in lead letters in the newspaper alongside yours, announcing your success. But now she is yours, and your worries can come to an end.

If she is pursued by several men at the same time, and the result is still that you capture her, then you are the victor in this love war. The glory on your face can truly shine with the gold ring on your finger, with extra prestige and spirit.

During leisure time, you can hold her arm and stroll around the busiest streets for a couple of laps, letting those single young men and women look at you, causing their irrelevant jealousy or envious "attention."

The most precious time in life is during the engagement. Once you get married, your good dreams gradually fade. The future life you imagined during your engagement is beautiful, sweet, and full of poetry. How considerate, gentle, affectionate, and comforting you will be to each other. But after marriage, how many loving couples are there in the world? You must try your best to enjoy your engagement life, and after getting engaged, don't rush to get married. This is my hope for those young men and women who are already engaged, but whether you listen or not is up to you. (My meaning is that such good dreams should be prolonged a little. You are eager to get married, only wanting to destroy this good dream.)

Because I myself have recently become engaged, I have many feelings in my heart, and I am also afraid that I am eager to destroy this good dream, so I wrote this article in a rambling way, to warn myself and to tell many people who wear engagement rings.

Let us stay in this good dream for a few more years!

The Singing of Autumn Insects 207

— Qing Qu

There are the most kinds of autumn insects. The ancients said, "Autumn is heralded by the singing of insects." This saying is indeed correct. Look, even before the weather has turned to autumn, the "Geges" (katydids) appear. People who make a living from this carry a load on their shoulders and stop on the streets, relying on these small insects to eat. It is said that they are all transported from the Zhenjiang area. If they are produced in Shandong, then their singing will be even louder! Actually, what is so good about this kind of singing? Moreover, the hotter the weather, the louder their sound. Alas! People who like to raise them not only do not find them annoying but say that listening to them can relieve the summer heat. I really don't understand.

Now that autumn has arrived, if you sit in front of the steps on a cool evening, hearing the sounds of the "Weaving Maid" and "Silk Reeler" (two kinds of insects, commonly known by these names in Jiading), you can be reminded of the principle that "if one woman does not weave, she may suffer from the cold," because their singing sounds very much like reeling silk and weaving cloth. It is a pity that the handicrafts in today's rural areas are truly not as diligent as they are! As for other insects like the "Bell" (divided into two types: heavenly bell and earthly bell, one being green and the other gray) and the "Jasmine Seed," those who are particular about it even use glass to glue together extremely ingenious boxes to keep them in. The heavenly bell is originally yin in nature, and when night falls, it becomes very active, flapping its wings and rubbing them together to make a sound. This sound is indeed clear and pleasant to listen to. Although the jasmine seed is small, when placed on the table, if you are flipping through books and reciting, its sound feels particularly quiet, and it constantly helps you with your pure enjoyment. Therefore, it is not right to say that autumn insects are completely without merit.

However, like crickets (which we in Jiading call "Zanji"), they are also autumn insects. You say they are different in nature? Hey! According to zoologists, all those who can produce beautiful sounds are male. They do so to pursue females and want to reproduce. There is no reason for people to raise them. Unexpectedly, people will use them as gambling tools. People move them left and right with a straw, and the winner crows triumphantly, while the loser is like falling flowers and flowing water, silent. It is really a sight to see. In fact, the cricket itself does not know that it is being fooled, which is most pitiful. Alas! It is not only autumn insects that are like this. I see that there are many people in the world who are doing this kind of dreaming!

Guidance 208

— Juan Yin

Unreasonable Reason 209

— (Wu Aibo)

Our dear compatriots, people say they don't know how to love their country. As I see it, this is a real injustice. There are facts to prove it:

I don't remember which day it was, but I took a tram to Hongkou. Several people got on halfway. The ticket seller asked them where they were going. One of them said: "Just the X station ahead, not far from here. This money is for you to enjoy." As he spoke, he held a large bag of copper coins in his hand, waved it in front of the ticket seller, and said: "We are all Chinese, everyone has to help each other." The ticket seller smiled and walked away.

Looking at it this way, who says we Chinese don't love our country?

Little Knowledge 210

— (Chu Yu)

Disinfecting Green Vegetables: The various green vegetables that we eat every day are often carriers of digestive infectious diseases because the cultivation of vegetables involves irrigating with human waste fertilizer, so the leaves and roots of the vegetables are attached with many infectious bacteria. In rural farmhouses, after cutting the vegetables, they are casually washed in streams or ponds and then brought to the cities to be sold. If they are washed and boiled before cooking, there is less danger. However, there are several kinds of vegetables that are eaten raw or are not completely boiled, so the infectious bacteria attached to the vegetable leaves can be very harmful. If we want to be safe, it is best to disinfect the green vegetables. The method of disinfection is to use bleaching powder (i.e., chloral lime). Bleaching powder is white, has a saltpetre smell, and turns red when dissolved in water. The effective ingredient of this powder only exerts its disinfecting power when 20-25% is decomposed in water. Because the disinfecting substance produced by decomposition is easily acidified (e.g., by organic matter and alkaline substances), it is still necessary to wash with clean water after washing with bleaching powder water, so that organic matter can be eliminated and the smell of bleaching powder can be washed away.

Simple Laundry Methods: Washing clothes differs depending on the material. The clothes worn in summer are mostly white silk crepe. Laundry shops use bleaching and steaming to wash silk clothes, but this is very inconvenient in ordinary households. Now there is a very simple method: use a basin of warm water, dissolve two scoops of washing soda, and soak the clothes thoroughly. Then, dirty things will easily fall off. After one or two hours, gently rub with your hands, take them out and wring them dry. Then, soak washing soap powder in boiling water, soak the clothes for an hour, take them out and slowly brush away stains with a scrubbing brush. If there are yellow stains, then bleaching should be used, which is to dissolve one scoop of bleaching powder in two quarts of cold water and soak the stained part. Stains will easily fall off. If the whole piece of silk is yellow, such as spun silk, which turns yellow after being worn for a long time, then two quarts of cold water, two scoops of bleaching powder, and one scoop of heavy alkali should be mixed and dissolved for soaking. However, cloth clothes should not be bleached. For Indian silk and thin silk crepe, one scoop of heavy alkali and one scoop of high-quality washing soap powder can be used. After washing, add one scoop of the vitriol, twenty drops of acetic acid, and one quart of water for washing. Then use two scoops of Hydrosalfit powder, five or six drops of acetic acid, and two quarts of boiling water to soak. When the material is pure white, take it out and rinse with clean water.

White Leather Shoe Refreshing Method: For leather shoes with white enamel on the leather surface, apply water oil first when buying them to prevent wrinkles and make the leather soft. After three or four days, wipe with vinegar. However, colored leather shoes will change color if wiped with vinegar. If there is dirty stuff stuck on the shoe surface, you can wipe it off with gasoline first. However, the most important thing to pay attention to when wearing white leather shoes is that if there is a stain, it should be cleaned up as soon as possible and should not be left for too long. If there is mud, brush off the mud first with a shoe brush, or rub with a rubber eraser, then wash with soapy water, apply white powder, and wait until it is dry before brushing all over with a hard-bristled shoe brush. The surface of ordinary white leather shoes is mostly made of white sheepskin, white deerskin, or white chamois skin, so it is easier to wash and scrub if they are not too dirty.

Chapter Eighteen: Qi Party's High Climb Flattering and Reproaching a Petty Official, Female Authority Runs Wild, Upsetting the Lady

Zhang Jiefu put away his worried look, forced a smile, and said, "Actually, even if Commissioner Lan doesn't come, my matter can also be published." Royal Fragrance Faintly Lingering Record 212

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

When the eunuch returned to the palace, my father asked him to bring me a secret letter, which roughly said:

"Since you have already agreed to the Empress Dowager, of course, I can't help but let you do it this time! But I must warn you that from now on, in the palace, you must keep two points firmly in mind: first, do not talk too much; second, do not boast of your abilities in front of people, thinking that you know more about everything than others, especially not in front of the Empress Dowager. Otherwise, I will really worry about you! I never expected that you remembered those French hair dyes so clearly. Wouldn't it be better if you had forgotten them earlier? If those medicines are sent and tried, and unfortunately damage the Empress Dowager's hair, I am afraid that the death penalty will undoubtedly be added to you! At that time, I will not have any power to save you, and I can only blame yourself for bringing it on!"

What my father said was of course good words, but in my mind at that time, my father was indeed too old-fashioned, daring not be careless about anything. I myself did not worry about anything and was very confident that my head would definitely not be cut off by the Empress Dowager because I firmly believed that those French hair dyes would definitely not be without effect. But after a long time, my experience increased, and I gradually realized that this kind of action was indeed like playing with fire and would cause a disaster if I were not careful.

More than forty days later, the Parisian hair dyes arrived as scheduled. As soon as I received them, I couldn't wait to hold those colorful boxes and send them to the Empress Dowager, and in front of her, I opened the boxes and took out a few bottles of medicine. At the same time, I said to her:

"There is also a very detailed instruction manual here! It teaches us how to use it, so we have to be careful to follow it..." (401)
